# What is Aster? | Aster

[Asterarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en)
 is a privacy-focused decentralized exchange, offering perpetual markets on crypto, stocks and commodities, and more commonly known as a perp DEX.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/#why-aster)

**Why Aster?**

Most perp DEXs make a trade-off you don't see until it costs you. On fully transparent platforms, every order, position size, and liquidation level is visible to anyone watching the chain. That information has value to other market participants, and they use it. Position hunting – where traders coordinate to push the market against a visible liquidation – has cost traders hundreds of millions of dollars. It's not a bug in how these platforms are run. It's a consequence of how they're built.

Aster is built to remove that dynamic. Every order is encrypted before it reaches the chain, decrypted only at execution, and never exposed in the order book. Your position size, entry point, and liquidation level stay yours. Privacy is the default.

This runs on Aster Chain, our own L1 built for private perps trading: 100,000+ transactions per second, 50ms block latency. The performance serious traders expect from a centralised exchange, with the self-custody and verifiability that only a DEX can offer.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/#explore-aster)

**Explore Aster**

Aster offers four seamless trading types:

*   [**Perpetuals**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
    : Perpetuals trading via an order book interface with deep liquidity, extremely low trading fees, and advanced trading tools.
    
*   [**Shield Mode:**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/trade/shield/futures/BTCUSDT)
     A simplified, AMM-style trading interface with built-in order and position privacy – faster, easier, and more streamlined, with higher leverage and a lower barrier to entry.
    
*   [**1001x**:arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/trade/1001x/futures/BTCUSD)
     Perp trading using onchain liquidity – one-click, MEV-resistant perp contract trading.
    
*   [**Spot**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/spot/ASTERUSDT)
    **:** Spot trading via an order book interface with deep liquidity, extremely low trading fees, and advanced trading tools.
    

Aster also provides yield products under Aster Earn, including the BNB liquid staking derivative asBNB and the yield-bearing stablecoin, USDF.

[NextRoadmapchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/overview/roadmap)

# Roadmap | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/overview/roadmap#key-recap-of-2025)

**Key Recap of 2025**

Before we unveil our next major focuses, let’s take a moment to celebrate the thrilling and extraordinary milestones Aster has accomplished this year. We extend our heartfelt gratitude to our incredible community. Your unwavering support has been the driving force behind every achievement.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FX0RQYpmxDQGHmc0fhuaQ%252FAster%25202025%2520Key%2520Milestones%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa5382d3-8c09-420d-a587-1c04c4cdb0ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db919702&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/overview/roadmap#three-foundational-engines-infrastructure-token-utility-and-ecosystem-and-community)

**Three Foundational Engines: Infrastructure, Token Utility, and Ecosystem & Community**

At Aster, everything begins with one simple belief: great products define great experiences. Our development is driven by three Foundational Engines: Infrastructure, Token Utility, and Ecosystem & Community.

These three engines form a continuous cycle: technology creates value, value fuels collaboration, and collaboration drives innovation. Together, they illustrate how Aster is evolving from a trading platform into a foundational layer of decentralized finance – each engine guided by its own set of detailed execution priorities.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fimbk7AGSPMLJ0S4d3TA5%252FAster%25E2%2580%2599s%2520Foundational%2520Engines%2520%285%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d0872bc-6cd8-4d45-8311-dedff1580d3d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79e4a96c&sv=2)

# Retrieving Incorrectly Deposited Assets | Aster

If you deposit the wrong tokens like USDC rather than USDT on the Arbitrum network, please follow the guidance to retrieve your tokens.

1.  Go to [https://www.asterdex.com/enarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en)
     and click \[Launch app\].
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FCAn6ve3eGK8ROQCINim3%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-13%252023.22.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D143661cb-5fff-4a5a-883e-3850580b7d07&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52772782&sv=2)

1.  Click the \[Connect\] button on the top right corner and enter your email address.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FIBf5dmPZ9UxUVc0Wls8a%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-13%252023.23.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a1337e3-57e1-461d-8c1f-94f6346ab388&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e3f6453&sv=2)

1.  Click the \[Withdraw\] button and check the third point.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FVjGpcmD6r7siK1K0Xebn%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-11-03%252011.39.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac902146-ce03-4dcf-a790-0b04682e2f34&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1e3900b&sv=2)

1.  Select the blockchain network (BNB, ETH, ARB or SOL) and token, input your destination address, and click \[Transfer\] button to retrieve your tokens.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2A9i3JRezTvCU8ccYerW%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-11-03%252011.41.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D915cacd9-2ceb-4cf6-8f39-75bf479ada46&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d8c9303&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/login-via-email-address/retrieving-incorrectly-deposited-assets#important-note)

**Important Note**

Users are responsible for paying gas fees when withdrawing unsupported assets from email-linked wallet to their wallet. Please make sure you have the corresponding tokens to pay gas fees for these networks:

*   BNB Chain: $BNB
    
*   Ethereum and Arbitrum: $ETH
    
*   Solana: $SOL

# Deposit & Withdrawal Guide | Aster

Before you can start trading on Aster, you need to transfer funds to your DEX account. This guide walks you through the deposit and withdrawal process.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#getting-started)

**Getting Started**

Start by connecting your wallet using the \[Connect wallet\] button in the top right corner of the interface.

Before you can start trading on Aster Pro, you need to transfer funds to your DEX account. This guide walks you through the deposit and withdrawal process.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#getting-started-1)

Getting Started

In [Aster Proarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
, connect your wallet by clicking \[Connect wallet\] button in the top right corner of the UI.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FZYUQmEnDwYgPuU3cAXQg%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-12%252015.46.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De80bec09-f1c9-454b-8c28-88093e69801c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1987c63&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#how-to-deposit)

**How to Deposit**

1.  Click the \[Deposit\] button
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F1kJfWQxoChp7krmRmoJ8%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-12%252015.50.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f103ee7-9238-4e0a-b484-03249929195d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5a08922&sv=2)

After a couple of minutes, your deposited balance will appear in your Portfolio.

2.  Click the \[Withdraw\] button
    
3.  Select the network, token, and amount to withdraw
    
4.  Approve the transfer in your wallet
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FvWw6sgQ3DfBiI1ktv7la%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-12%252015.53.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3169520e-84e3-49d4-b78e-5c6a62d4cb8e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4921403&sv=2)

1.  Select the network, token, and amount to withdraw
    
2.  Approve the transfer in your wallet
    

Your withdrawn funds will arrive in your wallet after a short wait.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#managing-negative-balances)

**Managing Negative Balances**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#why-negative-balances-occur)

**Why Negative Balances Occur**

The settlement asset for Aster is USDT. As multiple assets can be used as collateral, negative balances can result from:

*   Realized losses on closed positions
    
*   Funding fees
    
*   Trading commissions
    

You must resolve any negative balances before making withdrawals.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#why-negative-balances-occur-1)

Why Negative Balances Occur

The settlement asset for Aster Pro is USDT. Since Aster Pro supports multiple assets as collateral, negative balances can result from:

*   Realized losses on closed positions
    
*   Funding fees
    
*   Trading commissions
    

You must resolve any negative balances before making withdrawals.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FZvAoLm5HLSsHuinkai6l%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-06-17%252009.44.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D127ccb00-6a47-43d3-a728-4026e4a24a14&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a1da1df&sv=2)

An example of a negative balance

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#how-to-rebalance)

**How to Rebalance**

To fix a negative balance:

1.  Click \[Withdraw\] on the screen showing the token with a negative balance
    
2.  Click \[Rebalance\]
    

You can also manually deposit the exact token amount needed to cover the negative balance.

Rebalancing appears as "auto-conversion" in your transaction history.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide#how-to-rebalance-1)

**How to Rebalance**

To fix a negative balance:

2.  Click \[Rebalance\]

Rebalancing appears as "auto-conversion" in your transaction history.

# Login via Web3 Wallet | Aster

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/login-via-web3-wallet#connecting-your-wallet)

Connecting Your Wallet


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start trading on Aster, you need to connect a compatible Web3 wallet.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/login-via-web3-wallet#supported-wallets)

Supported Wallets

Aster supports Rabby, MetaMask, Binance Wallet, and any wallet compatible with WalletConnect.

**Note:** If connecting to BNB Chain, your wallet must hold at least 0.001 BNB.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/login-via-web3-wallet#steps)

Steps

1.  Go to [asterdex.comarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en)
     and click **\[Launch App\]**.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FvE7E7j5N5y2HwIGoMibb%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252015.29.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd55cb64e-e9e9-47f8-ac35-1deeb10761b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6301895f&sv=2)

1.  Select your chain from the dropdown menu, then click **\[Connect Wallet\]**.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FHvrHynSXyfROjO7d8lOp%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252015.32.30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9678c7de-d88f-4ca5-8f89-22b282461059&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d642c12&sv=2)

1.  Choose your wallet.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FHRklRpUJ0cxMNn5YvCdz%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252015.34.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35a441f0-acdc-42f4-811b-0af8b911d62a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aae8ebd&sv=2)

1.  A signature request will appear in your wallet. Approve it to complete the connection.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F0Jqp95GDz5GWqWnj4k0e%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252015.35.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0baa5877-d13d-4d5c-9785-e26be96bd200&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3d60a83&sv=2)

# Login via Email Address | Aster

Aster supports email login for your convenience. All you need is a valid email address – once you've deposited funds, you'll be ready to use Aster's products.

**Note:** Email login currently only supports USDT deposits on the Arbitrum network.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/login-via-email-address#steps)

**Steps**

1.  Go to [https://www.asterdex.com/enarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en)
     and click **\[Launch app\]**.
    
    ![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FvE7E7j5N5y2HwIGoMibb%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252015.29.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd55cb64e-e9e9-47f8-ac35-1deeb10761b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6301895f&sv=2)
    
2.  Click the **\[Connect\]** button in the top right corner and enter your email address.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FFX90RN6IBSmWgfNshJ1n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d3734ee-6796-4f3c-ae2c-d8762cf7326d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f5ad4c&sv=2)

1.  A 6-digit verification code will be sent to your email. Enter the code to log in.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FklALIyYeKiaKPkDP8i54%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a874fda-ede4-4243-a5a9-42f453ebc943&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96fcd680&sv=2)

1.  Create and enter a strong password for your Aster account.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FkVwhIJM7LotV3rUb7tyN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5417b130-47ed-4892-b693-7aa9d5577304&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b07f672&sv=2)

1.  Sign the popup message.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fjr0znpjA9dkU9bNihjiX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fb935e5-a271-46ac-9e5c-ffdd87846c0f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3ff679b&sv=2)

1.  A new wallet address will be generated for your email. Click the **\[Deposit\]** button – accessible from your wallet address in the top right corner – to fund your account.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F7m0VvP8x2grNNWCsd950%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b953ebb-63e0-4e3d-830f-ac3673c695f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2961679c&sv=2)

1.  Deposit collateral from your Web3 wallet or a centralized exchange (CEX) using a supported network. **You can only deposit USDT via the** [**Arbitrum One**arrow-up-right](https://arbitrum.io/)
     **to your email-linked wallet. Aster is not liable for refunds if you deposit the wrong asset or use the wrong network.**
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FCT1mmyG7EXvo1a6iHKPB%252FFrame%25201312315515.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70ed51d4-e1fc-44b0-ba71-d259b00095a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0e9f485&sv=2)

1.  Once your wallet receives USDT on Arbitrum, you can use it as collateral to trade on Aster.

[NextRetrieving Incorrectly Deposited Assetschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/login-via-email-address/retrieving-incorrectly-deposited-assets)

# Troubleshooting WalletConnect | Aster

If you're experiencing issues connecting your wallet to Aster Mobile through WalletConnect, this guide covers the most common problems and their solutions. Most connection issues can be resolved by reconnecting your wallet.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview/troubleshooting-walletconnect#error-given-link-couldnt-be-opened)

**Error: "Given link couldn't be opened"**

**Problem:** You tap your wallet but receive an error message saying the link couldn't be opened.

**Solution:** Make sure you have the wallet app installed on your phone. WalletConnect uses app deep linking – if the compatible wallet app isn't installed, the connection will fail.

**Fix:**

1.  Install the supported wallet app
    
2.  Try connecting again
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview/troubleshooting-walletconnect#wallet-opens-but-no-connection-prompt-appears)

**Wallet Opens but No Connection Prompt Appears**

**Problem:** Your wallet app opens, but it doesn't show a prompt asking you to approve the connection.

**Solution:** This sometimes happens due to a temporary glitch with WalletConnect. Force-closing both apps and reconnecting usually resolves the issue.

**Fix:**

1.  Force-close both Aster Mobile and your wallet app
    
2.  Reopen Aster Mobile and try connecting again
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview/troubleshooting-walletconnect#wallet-doesnt-open-or-switch-back-to-aster-mobile)

**Wallet Doesn't Open or Switch Back to Aster Mobile**

**Problem:** The apps aren't automatically switching back and forth during the connection or signature process.

**Solution:** WalletConnect doesn't always automatically switch between apps, especially on certain devices. You may need to manually return to each app to complete the steps.

**Fix:**

Manually switch back to Aster Mobile or your wallet to complete the current step.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview/troubleshooting-walletconnect#wallet-accounts-not-switching)

**Wallet Accounts Not Switching**

**Problem:** Changing your wallet account or network doesn't update in Aster Mobile.

**Solution:** WalletConnect sessions are tied to the specific account and network you originally approved. Changing either inside your wallet doesn't automatically update your Aster Mobile session.

**Fix:**

1.  Disconnect your wallet from Aster Mobile
    
2.  Reconnect using your desired account and network
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview/troubleshooting-walletconnect#still-having-issues)

**Still Having Issues?**

If none of these solutions work, reach out to the Aster community on Discord for additional support.

# Aster Mobile App Overview | Aster

Download Aster Mobile by tapping ["Download beta"arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en)
 on the Aster website.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview#getting-started-with-the-aster-app)

**Getting Started with the Aster App**

Follow these steps to connect your wallet and start trading:

1.  Open the app and tap \[Connect wallet\] at the top right
    
2.  Tap \[Connect\] again to proceed
    
3.  Select your preferred blockchain network
    
4.  Choose your wallet. If you don’t have one, we recommend using [**Trust Wallet**arrow-up-right](https://trustwallet.com/?utm_source=cryptwerk)
    .
    
5.  Approve the connection request in your wallet app
    
6.  Approve the signature request to complete the connection
    

You're all set! You can now start using the Aster App to trade perps.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/getting-started/aster-mobile-app-overview#getting-started-with-the-aster-app-1)

Getting Started with the Aster App

Follow these steps to connect your wallet and start trading:

1.  Open the app and tap \[Connect wallet\] at the top right
    
2.  Tap \[Connect\] again to proceed
    
3.  Select your preferred blockchain network
    
4.  Choose your wallet If you don't have one, we recommend using [Trust Walletarrow-up-right](https://trustwallet.com/?utm_source=cryptwerk)
    
5.  Approve the connection request in your wallet app
    
6.  Approve the signature request to complete the connection
    

You're all set! You can now start using the Aster App to trade perps.

# Overview | Aster

At the heart of the Aster ecosystem is the $ASTER token, a core asset that secures the network, decentralizes governance, drives growth, rewards participation, and supports long-term sustainability.

*   **Ticker:** $ASTER
    
*   **Maximum Supply:** 8,000,000,000
    
*   **Token Standard:** BEP-20 on BNB Chain
    
*   **Token address:** 0x000Ae314E2A2172a039B26378814C252734f556A

# Tokenomics | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#allocation-and-distribution-schedule)

**Allocation and Distribution Schedule**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#token-allocation)

**Token Allocation**

The $ASTER token supply is distributed across several key categories to support community growth, ecosystem development, and long-term protocol sustainability.

**Category**

**Description**

**Allocation**

Airdrop

Incentives for traders, community builders, and key ecosystem stakeholders

53.5%

Ecosystem & Community

Migration pool for APX holders, ecosystem grants, marketing initiatives, initial liquidity and staking rewards on exchanges

30%

Treasury

Reserved for future strategic initiatives, operational reserves, and governance flexibility

7%

Team

Allocated to Aster core contributors and advisors with cliff vesting

5%

Liquidity & Listings

Reserved for exchange listings to facilitate liquidity bootstrapping.

4.5%

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2e9y8dXGVPthkgOpyZro%252FTGE_%2524ASTER%2520token%2520allocation%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa32e06a-b86d-4917-8a0a-0c032f5ee72b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9345e295&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#airdrop-53.5-4-280-000-000-usdaster)

**Airdrop (53.5% - 4,280,000,000 $ASTER)**

8.8% of total allocation (704,000,000 $ASTER) will be unlocked immediately upon Aster TGE for eligible participants from two reward programs: Aster Spectra and Aster Gems.

Unclaimed $ASTER tokens will be redirected back to Airdrop & Community Rewards allocation for future community distribution.

All remaining $ASTER tokens under this category will be gradually released over the next 80 months (approximately 7 years), subject to future adjustments by protocol governance.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#ecosystem-and-community-30-2-400-000-000-usdaster)

**Ecosystem & Community (30% - 2,400,000,000 $ASTER)**

The APX Upgrade, Marketing & Ecosystem allocation is reserved for APX upgrade allocation, liquidity bootstrapping, ecosystem partnerships, staking rewards and grants.

Eligible $APX holders and stakers will be able to exchange their tokens for $ASTER during a designated swap period. The conversion rate will decrease over time.

This allocation (excluding the APX to ASTER swap) was originally vested over 20 months on a linear distribution model. The linear vesting was active for 4 months (October 2025 – January 2026) and has since been replaced by a staking emission model. Staking rewards are currently the sole active use of this allocation. Refer to the Staking page for current emission parameters.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#treasury-7-560-000-000-usdaster)

**Treasury (7% - 560,000,000 $ASTER)**

The Foundation Treasury allocation is reserved for future strategic growth initiatives, operational reserves, and governance initiatives.

It will not enter circulating supply after TGE and remains fully locked until utilized via governance-approved mechanisms.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#team-5-400-000-000-usdaster)

**Team (5% - 400,000,000 $ASTER)**

The Team & Advisors allocation is reserved for the long-term alignment of core contributors and advisors.

*   **Cliff:** 12 months from TGE
    
*   **Vesting**: 40 months of linear distribution (10,000,000 $ASTER per month)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#liquidity-and-listing-4.5-360-000-000-usdaster)

**Liquidity & Listing (4.5% - 360,000,000 $ASTER)**

The Liquidity & Listing allocation is reserved for exchange listings to facilitate liquidity bootstrapping. This allocation will be fully unlocked upon TGE.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#overall-highlights)

**Overall Highlights**

*   53.5% of $ASTER is reserved for community rewards via airdrops.
    
*   A total of 704,000,000 $ASTER (8.8% of total supply) will be fully unlocked immediately upon TGE for users who participated in the Aster Spectra program and other initiatives.
    
*   $APX holders upgrade to $ASTER tokens. The conversion rate will decrease over time. Unclaimed tokens will be redirected into the Airdrop pool for future rewards.
    
*   Remaining $ASTER will be distributed gradually over time for long-term protocol sustainability.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster-token/tokenomics#protocol-revenue-buyback-initiative)

**Protocol Revenue Buyback Initiative**

To celebrate the official launch of $ASTER, a portion of protocol revenue will be used for $ASTER buybacks:

*   Aster Foundation allocation for long-term stabilization buyback
    
*   Governance rewards distribution to incentivize participation in Aster's decentralized governance system

# Frequently Asked Questions | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-1.-why-do-i-need-to-choose-both-a-validator-and-a-lock-period-when-staking)

**1\. Why do I need to choose both a validator and a lock period when staking?**

Aster Chain staking distributes rewards through two layers. The validator you select determines your Base APY, while the lock period determines your Loyalty Rewards weight. Both choices work together to determine your total staking rewards.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-2.-does-a-new-stake-start-earning-rewards-immediately)

**2\. Does a new stake start earning rewards immediately?**

No. New stakes, additional deposits, and lock extensions typically begin earning rewards from the next epoch.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-3.-are-rewards-distributed-in-real-time)

**3\. Are rewards distributed in real time?**

No. Rewards are settled once per Epoch, which currently occurs on a weekly basis. Each Epoch is seven days, running from Monday at 00:00 UTC to Sunday at 23:59 UTC.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-4.-what-factors-affect-my-staking-rewards)

**4\. What factors affect my staking rewards?**

Your total rewards depend on several factors, including:

*   The validator's transaction contribution
    
*   The validator's commission rate
    
*   Your share of the total stake within the validator
    
*   Your lock period
    
*   Your veASTER weight
    
*   Network-wide staking participation and total Power
    

Because rewards are distributed proportionally, actual returns may vary depending on overall network conditions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-5.-can-i-add-more-usdaster-to-an-existing-staking-position)

**5\. Can I add more $ASTER to an existing staking position?**

Yes. You can increase your stake at any time. However, all staking positions share a unified lock period, meaning newly added tokens must follow the same unlock schedule as your existing stake.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-6.-can-i-extend-my-lock-period)

**6\. Can I extend my lock period?**

Yes. You may extend your lock duration to increase your veASTER weight, which can increase your share of Loyalty Rewards. When the lock period is extended, the new unlock date applies to your entire staking position.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-7.-can-i-switch-validators-during-staking)

**7\. Can I switch validators during staking?**

Yes. Users can switch their delegated stake to a different validator at any time. The change takes effect in the next Epoch, after which rewards will begin accruing from the new validator.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-8.-can-i-exit-staking-early)

**8\. Can I exit staking early?**

Yes. Users may request to unlock their stake before the lock period ends. However, early exits trigger a penalty, which increases with the amount of time remaining in the lock period.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-9.-what-happens-to-penalized-tokens)

**9\. What happens to penalized tokens?**

Penalized tokens are redistributed according to protocol rules. A portion is added to future staking reward pools, while another portion is allocated to the ecosystem fund.

This mechanism discourages short-term staking while benefiting long-term participants.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-10.-will-i-be-penalized-if-i-exit-after-the-lock-period-ends)

**10\. Will I be penalized if I exit after the lock period ends?**

No. If you exit staking at or after the scheduled unlock time, no penalty is applied. Your principal and accumulated rewards can be withdrawn normally.

[PreviousEarly Exit Mechanismchevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/early-exit-mechanism)
[NextTestnetchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/testnet)

Last updated 22 days ago

*   [2\. Does a new stake start earning rewards immediately?](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-2.-does-a-new-stake-start-earning-rewards-immediately)
    
*   [3\. Are rewards distributed in real time?](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-3.-are-rewards-distributed-in-real-time)
    
*   [4\. What factors affect my staking rewards?](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions#id-4.-what-factors-affect-my-staking-rewards)

# Early Exit Mechanism | Aster

Users may exit before the lock period ends, but doing so triggers a penalty. The penalty depends on how much time remains before the original unlock date.

**Penalty formula:**

`Penalty Amount = unlockAmount × max(N%, min(M%, lock_duration_left ÷ 4 years))`

**Where:**

**Parameter**

**Meaning**

unlockAmount

Principal to withdraw

lock\_duration\_left

Remaining lock duration

M%

Maximum penalty rate (example: 60%)

N%

Minimum penalty rate (example: 2%)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/early-exit-mechanism#penalty-examples)

**Penalty Examples**

**Assuming:**

Stake = 10,000 ASTER ,Maximum penalty = 60% ,Minimum penalty = 2%

**Scenario**

**Remaining Lock**

**Penalty Rate**

**Penalty Amount**

Exit immediately

4 years

60%

6,000 $ASTER

Exit after 1 year

3 years

60%

6,000 $ASTER

Exit after 2 years

2 years

50%

5,000 $ASTER

Exit after 3 years

1 year

25%

2,500 $ASTER

Exit near maturity

0.05 years

2%

200 $ASTER

Exit at maturity

0

0%

0 $ASTER

**Net withdrawal amount:**

`Net Amount = Principal − Penalty Amount + Accumulated Rewards`

Penalized tokens are redistributed according to protocol rules:

*   A portion enters the next epoch reward pool
    
*   A portion goes to the ecosystem fund
    

[PreviousHow Staking Workschevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works)
[NextFrequently Asked Questionschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/frequently-asked-questions)

# Testnet | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/testnet#what-is-the-aster-testnet)

**What is the Aster Testnet?**

The Aster Testnet is a blockchain network established solely for testing new features and products for Aster users. No tokens — or trades made — on the testnet have any financial value.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/testnet#how-to-use-the-aster-testnet)

**How to use the Aster Testnet**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/testnet#accessing-the-testnet)

**Accessing the Testnet**

You can access the Testnet via [www.asterdex-testnet.comarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex-testnet.com/)
.

The default network is **BNB Chain Testnet**. Please make sure your wallet supports BNB Chain Testnet before proceeding.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FCloQp6rWoaJL7660SwV3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3fe43c37-f3ee-415f-8f9b-eceb8b282c12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56ccd53c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/testnet#permission-and-whitelist-access)

**Permission & Whitelist Access**

Currently, only officially invited whitelist users are allowed to trade on the Testnet.

To request whitelist access, visit [Discord Channelarrow-up-right](https://discord.com/channels/1239477531128631317/1452552068987486222)
 and contact the Aster team for an invitation.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/testnet#get-testnet-tokens)

Get Testnet Tokens

Whitelist users can claim Testnet tokens from the [Faucet pagearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex-testnet.com/en/faucet)
.

Each whitelisted user can claim:

*   1,000 USDT (Testnet)
    
*   1,000 ASTER (Testnet)
    

Token claims are available **once per day.**

# Overview | Aster

Aster Chain is a high-performance, privacy-focused Layer 1 blockchain designed specifically for derivatives trading.

It powers Aster DEX, enabling a decentralized exchange environment where traders retain full custody of their assets and benefit from strong privacy protections while experiencing execution speeds comparable to centralized exchanges. Aster Chain enables millisecond-level performance without sacrificing decentralization or transparency.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#consensus-mechanism-posa)

**Consensus Mechanism (PoSA)**

Aster Chain uses **PoSA (Proof-of-Staked Authority)** as its consensus mechanism.

PoSA is a hybrid model that combines:

*   **Proof of Stake (PoS)** economic incentives
    
*   **Proof of Authority (PoA)** validator reputation systems
    

This design allows the network to achieve fast execution while maintaining:

*   Transparency
    
*   High throughput
    
*   Decentralization
    

All order matching and trading logic are ultimately processed and stored **onchain**, aligning with the long-term goal of building a **fully decentralized derivatives infrastructure**.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#top-tier-performance)

**Top-Tier Performance**

Aster Chain is optimized for ultra-low latency trading environments.

Through the combination of **PoSA consensus**, integrated node aggregation engines, and block pre-confirmation mechanisms, the network achieves:

*   **Block time**: 50 ms
    
*   **Transaction Per Second (TPS)**: up to 100,000 TPS
    
*   **Gas fees**: 0
    

This performance enables Aster to deliver a trading experience comparable to centralized exchanges while preserving decentralized settlement and verification.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#transparent-yet-private)

**Transparent Yet Private**

Aster Chain provides built-in privacy protection for trader activity. When Account Privacy is off, all trader activity is published onchain and publicly visible.

**Account Privacy:** The default setting for all users, where asset balances and open positions are hidden from public view. Account Privacy is powered by two complementary mechanisms:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#zk-verifiable-encrypted-orders)

**ZK-Verifiable Encrypted Orders**

Every order placed under Account Privacy is encrypted and verifiable using Zero-Knowledge (ZK) cryptography. Trades do not appear directly in the transaction history of the trader's primary address. The underlying order data is never exposed onchain in plaintext.

Users can verify their complete transaction history at any time by providing their viewer pass, which allows selective disclosure without revealing data to third parties.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#stealth-address-mechanism)

**Stealth Address Mechanism**

Each trade under Account Privacy automatically generates a fresh, one-time stealth address for that transaction. A single user accumulates many ephemeral addresses over time, each used only once.

External observers cannot link these addresses back to the trader's real account or correlate activity across transactions.

This makes onchain tracking and behavioral analysis effectively impossible without the trader's viewer pass.

_Note: Hidden orders always require ZK verification regardless of whether Account Privacy is on or off. To comply with regulatory requirements, internal transfers to other users are not permitted while Account Privacy is active._

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#transparency)

**Transparency**

Aster Chain maintains a dedicated block explorer that supports both standard and privacy-aware queries:

*   Query assets, positions, blocks, hashes, and transactions.
    

When Account Privacy is on, trader activity is not publicly displayed.

Users can verify their own private transactions – or those of other traders – via **ZK proof**, provided the viewer pass is supplied.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#cross-chain-interoperability)

**Cross-Chain Interoperability**

Aster Chain is designed to interact seamlessly with multiple major blockchains.

Supported networks include:

*   BNB Chain
    
*   Ethereum
    
*   Arbitrum
    
*   Solana
    

The long-term goal is to support cross-chain perpetual trading and unify liquidity across multiple ecosystems.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#blockchain-explorer)

**Blockchain Explorer**

Aster Chain provides a dedicated blockchain explorer for network transparency.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#core-functions)

**Core Functions**

Users can:

*   View asset balances and account activity
    
*   Query blocks, transactions, and hashes
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#privacy-protection)

**Privacy Protection**

When Account Privacy is on:

*   Trader activity is not publicly displayed
    
*   Users may verify their own private transactions using **Zero-Knowledge verification**. Verification of other trader’s private transactions requires a **viewer pass**.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#cross-chain-deposits-and-withdrawals)

Cross-Chain Deposits & Withdrawals

Aster Chain provides a secure cross-chain bridge system.

All bridge operations:

*   Are validator-signed
    
*   Can be verified onchain
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#smart-contracts-and-open-source-policy)

**Smart Contracts & Open Source Policy**

Bridge contracts and related code will be publicly disclosed on the **Smart Contracts page**.

However:

*   Core chain contracts and RPC infrastructure will not be open-sourced at the moment
    

This approach is designed to:

*   Protect proprietary matching engine algorithms
    
*   Improve network security during early deployment stages
    

Despite partial closed-source components, the ZK architecture ensures trust minimization and censorship resistance.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#validator-participation)

**Validator Participation**

During Phase 1, external validator participation is not supported.

As the ecosystem grows, Aster plans to gradually introduce:

*   Observer nodes
    
*   Staking validators
    

The long-term architecture aims to expand decentralization while maintaining high performance.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#deposits)

**Deposits**

Cross-chain deposits are processed once 3 out of 4 validator nodes verify the transaction.

*   Deposit fee on Aster Chain: 0
    
*   Estimated arrival time: 1–5 minutes
    
*   Ethereum deposits may take longer depending on block production and gas conditions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#withdrawals)

**Withdrawals**

Withdrawals are processed in batched transactions. A withdrawal is confirmed once 2 out of 3 validator nodes verify the request.

Key characteristics:

*   Gas fees apply to cover validator operational costs
    
*   Fees are calculated based on the destination chain
    
*   Minimum withdrawal fee may be as low as 1 USDT
    

Estimated withdrawal time:

*   ~30 seconds
    
*   Ethereum withdrawals may take longer depending on network conditions.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#oracle-system)

**Oracle System**

Each validator calculates a weighted median spot price using data from 14 major exchanges:

*   Binance
    
*   HTX
    
*   HitBTC
    
*   Gate.io
    
*   Poloniex
    
*   OKX
    
*   KuCoin
    
*   AscendEX
    
*   MEXC
    
*   Bitfinex
    
*   Coinbase
    
*   Bitstamp
    
*   Kraken
    
*   Bybit
    

Oracle prices are updated in real time and are used for:

*   Funding rate calculations
    
*   Mark price determination
    
*   Triggering TP/SL orders
    

For liquidation, the system uses the median oracle price weighted by validator stake.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#clearinghouse)

**Clearinghouse**

The Clearinghouse is the core execution component of Aster Chain.

It manages for each trader:

*   Status of margin balances
    
*   Open positions
    

Each perpetual market operates with an independent **order book**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#margin-management)

**Margin Management**

Deposits first enter the user’s cross margin balance. By default, all positions open in cross margin mode.

Traders may switch to isolated margin to limit the risk exposure of a specific position.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#cross-margin)

**Cross Margin**

All positions share a common margin pool.

Profits and losses are aggregated across the account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#isolated-margin)

**Isolated Margin**

Each position maintains independent margin. Liquidation risk is limited to that specific position.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview#data-storage)

**Data Storage**

Aster Chain prioritizes transparency while maintaining privacy compatibility.

Key trading and account events are recorded onchain, while certain operations remain offchain for privacy protection and system efficiency.

# Staking | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking#overview)

**Overview**

Delegate $ASTER to Aster Chain validators and earn rewards.

When staking, users make two key choices:

*   Select a validator
    
*   Choose a lock period
    

These two choices determine how rewards are generated and distributed.

The basic staking flow can be summarized as:

Select a validator → Stake $ASTER → Choose a lock period → Earn epoch rewards

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking#what-is-a-validator)

**What is a Validator?**

A validator is responsible for processing transactions and producing blocks on Aster Chain.

When users stake $ASTER, they delegate their tokens to a validator. Each validator contributes differently to the network, and this performance determines the validator's total rewards.

Once the rewards are received, they are shared proportionally among delegators after deducting the validator's commission.

This design ensures validators compete based on real network contribution rather than simply attracting large amounts of stake.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking#what-is-the-lock-period)

**What is the Lock Period?**

The lock period is the duration where the staked $ASTER cannot be withdrawn without penalty. It determines your Loyalty Rewards weight, and a longer lock period means greater reward weight.

The current **maximum lock duration is 208 weeks (approximately 4 years).**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking#dual-reward-structure)

**Dual Reward Structure**

Aster Chain staking distributes rewards through two distinct layers.

**Reward Layer**

**Determined By**

**Weekly Reward Pool**

Base APY

Validator transaction share and your delegation size

150,000 $ASTER

Loyalty Rewards

Lock duration and trading activity

300,000 $ASTER

Separating these two reward streams serves two goals:

*   Encouraging healthy competition between validators
    
*   Incentivizing long-term staking commitment
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking#key-terms)

**Key Terms**

**Term**

**Description**

$ASTER

Native token used for staking, rewards, and governance

Validator

Validator receiving delegated stake

Delegation

Relationship between user and validator

Lock Position

The staking position tied to a lock duration

Epoch

Reward settlement cycle (currently weekly)

Base APY

Yield derived from validator performance

Loyalty Rewards

Additional yield based on long-term lock commitment

veASTER

Weight metric derived from locked ASTER and lock duration

Power

Loyalty reward weight calculated from veASTER and Trading Volume Boost

Total Power

Combined Power of all users in a given Epoch

Penalty

Penalty applied for exiting before the lock period ends

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/overview)
[NextHow Staking Workschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works)

# How Staking Works | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#creating-a-staking-position)

Creating a Staking Position

To participate in staking:

1.  Connect your wallet and navigate to the [staking pagearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/staking)
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FhD4cLj2Odb59ZvXvD8Ai%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2026-03-20%252015.47.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02521d3b-8ac6-4df5-be33-c811552bda23&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd6b917a&sv=2)

1.  Select a validator and click Stake button
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fm4KvHlFQs0z4O2Jp8382%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2026-03-20%252015.48.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde0c7d43-743f-4958-b117-f578fca8a9ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b2a314&sv=2)

1.  Enter the amount of $ASTER to stake
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FWYqMQTAKSlreqAyRiFn5%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2026-03-20%252015.50.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb30a92b-aa5b-4e8b-971b-11e5abae1304&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ef2e363&sv=2)

1.  Choose a lock period
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FK8ALuuTtUDC3utTOC09V%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2026-03-20%252015.50.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0a684d0-cd67-4e3b-ae53-7bcf45aecc59&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f84df7&sv=2)

1.  Confirm the transaction
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FClLBBa2o56ttOKXksv1r%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2026-03-20%252015.52.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68b549bb-6e43-46c1-9f2f-896e41d500a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52bf3320&sv=2)

Once confirmed, the staking position becomes active and begins earning rewards in future Epochs.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#rewards-pool-per-epoch)

**Rewards Pool per Epoch**

Emissions per Epoch at launch:

*   Base Rewards pool: 150,000 $ASTER
    
*   Loyalty Rewards pool: 300,000 $ASTER
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#base-apy)

**Base APY**

Base APY is the foundational reward layer tied to validator performance. Each validator receives a share of the Base APY pool proportional to the transactions it processes.

**Validator reward calculation:**

Validator Share = Validator Transactions ÷ Total Network Transactions

Validator Reward = Base APY Pool × Validator Share

**Example:**

If the Base APY pool is 100 $ASTER and a validator processes 40% of network transactions:

Validator Reward = 100 × 40% = 40 ASTER

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#your-share-of-base-apy)

**Your Share of Base APY**

After the validator receives its reward, users earn proportionally based on their stake within that validator.

**User Base Reward Formula:**

User Reward = Validator Reward × (User Stake ÷ Total Validator Stake) × (1 − Validator Commission)

**Example:**

**Parameter**

**Value**

Validator Reward

40

Total Validator Stake

10,000,000 $ASTER

User Stake

500,000 $ASTER

Commission

10%

User stake ratio = 500,000 ÷ 10,000,000 = **5%**

After commission = 5% × (1 − 10%) = **4.5%**

User reward = 40 × 4.5% = **1.8 ASTER**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#loyalty-rewards)

**Loyalty Rewards**

Loyalty Rewards are designed to reward long-term commitment. The longer you lock, the more you earn.

Reward weight is determined using veASTER and a Trading Volume Boost.

**Power formula:**

Power = veASTER × Boost

**Where:**

veASTER = Locked Amount × Time Weight

Time Weight = Remaining Lock Duration ÷ Maximum Lock Duration

Maximum lock duration = 208 weeks (approximately 4 years)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#trading-volume-boost)

**Trading Volume Boost**

Your reward weight can be boosted based on your personal trading volume within each Epoch.

**Your Epoch Trading Volume**

**Boost**

\> 500K

1.05

\> 50M

1.15

\> 200M

1.25

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#loyalty-rewards-distribution)

**Loyalty Rewards Distribution**

Loyalty Rewards are distributed proportionally based on Power share.

**User Weekly Reward:**

User Reward = Weekly Loyalty Pool × (User Power ÷ Total Network Power)

**Example:**

**Parameter**

**Value**

Weekly Loyalty Pool

100,000 $ASTER

Total Network Power

1,000,000

User Power

5,000

User share = 5,000 ÷ 1,000,000 = **0.5%**

User reward = 100,000 × 0.5% = **500 $ASTER**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/aster-chain/staking/how-staking-works#epoch-settlement)

**Epoch Settlement**

Rewards are calculated and distributed using weekly Epoch cycles. Each Epoch runs Monday through Sunday. A snapshot of staking data is taken at Monday 00:00 UTC.

**Event**

**Timing**

Epoch Start

Monday 00:00 UTC

Snapshot

Monday 00:00 UTC

Settlement

Sunday 00:00 UTC

Operations that take effect in the next Epoch include:

*   New stake deposits
    
*   Additional stake top-ups
    
*   Lock extensions
    
*   Redeem requests

# Calculating Maximum Transfers in Cross and Isolated Margin | Aster

When using Cross or Isolated Margin modes, the amount you can transfer in or out depends on your wallet balance, margin requirements, and unrealized PnL.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin/calculating-maximum-transfers-in-cross-and-isolated-margin#cross-margin)

**Cross Margin**

In Cross Margin mode, your margin balance is shared across all open positions.

**If there is no unrealized PnL:**

Maximum transferable amount = Cross wallet balance − Σ(Isolated open order initial margin) − Σ(Cross position maintenance margin)

**If there is unrealized PnL:**

Maximum transferable amount = Cross wallet balance + Σ(Cross unrealized PnL) − Σ(Cross initial margin) − Σ(Isolated open order initial margin)

**Note:** These calculations assume no gift balance or cross collateral.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin/calculating-maximum-transfers-in-cross-and-isolated-margin#isolated-margin)

**Isolated Margin**

In Isolated Margin mode, margin is dedicated to each individual position.

**Maximum transfer-in amount for Isolated Margin:**

Maximum transfer-in amount = min (Cross wallet balance − Σ(Isolated open position initial margin) − Σ(Cross position maintenance margin), Available balance)

**Maximum transfer-out amount for Isolated Margin:**

Maximum transfer-out amount = max (0, min (Isolated wallet balance − Isolated position maintenance margin,

Isolated wallet balance + Size × (Mark price − Entry price) − Mark price × Abs(Size) × Initial margin rate))

**Note:** Transferring margin out reduces the buffer protecting your position. Removing too much margin can increase your risk of liquidation.

[PreviousMarginchevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin)
[NextSingle-Asset Mode & Multi-Asset Modechevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/single-asset-mode-and-multi-asset-mode)

Last updated 23 days ago

*   [Cross Margin](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin/calculating-maximum-transfers-in-cross-and-isolated-margin#cross-margin)
    
*   [Isolated Margin](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin/calculating-maximum-transfers-in-cross-and-isolated-margin#isolated-margin)

# Perpetuals | Aster

[**Aster Perpetuals**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/trade/pro/futures/BTCUSDT)
**,** or simply Perps, is Aster’s decentralized perpetual contracts product and the core of our platform. It's designed to give traders greater control, deeper functionality, and a full suite of tools for advanced strategies. Perps are available on all supported chains on Aster.

This section covers everything you need to trade perps effectively — including trading mechanics, margin systems, risk management tools, and more.

This section covers everything you need to use Pro effectively – including trading mechanics, margin systems, risk management tools, and more.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals#key-features)

**Key Features**

*   Multi-asset mode: Trade using a variety of cryptocurrencies as margin
    
*   Lower-than-CEX fees: 0.01% maker fee, 0.035% taker fee

# Margin | Aster

Margin trading on Aster Perps lets you amplify your positions by using leverage, allowing you to trade with more size than your actual balance.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin#leverage)

**Leverage**

Leverage lets you open a larger position with a smaller amount of collateral. For example, with 10× leverage, a $100 margin allows you to open a $1,000 position.

You can set your desired leverage using the slider or input field in the trading panel. Each asset has its own maximum leverage limit.

The initial margin required to open a position is calculated as:

(Position size × Mark price) / Leverage

Leverage lets you open a larger position with a smaller amount of collateral. For example, with 10× leverage, a $100 margin allows you to open a $1,000 position.

You can set your desired leverage using the slider or input field in the trading panel. Each asset has its own maximum leverage limit.

The initial margin required to open a position is calculated as:

(Position size × Mark price) / Leverage

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin#margin-modes)

**Margin Modes**

Aster supports two margin modes:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin#cross-margin-default)

**Cross Margin (default)**

Your margin is shared across all open positions. Profits from one trade can offset losses in another, reducing liquidation risk – but your entire margin balance is at stake.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin#isolated-margin)

**Isolated Margin**

Margin is applied to a single position only. If the trade moves against you, only the margin tied to that position is at risk; other positions remain unaffected.

You can select the margin mode in the trading interface (Cross/Isolated) before opening a position. You cannot change the margin mode after submitting a position or placing an open order.

You can select the margin mode in the trading interface (Cross/Isolated) before opening a position. You cannot change the margin mode after submitting a position or placing an open order.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin#monitoring-margin)

**Monitoring Margin**

Your used margin, liquidation price, and available balance are displayed in real time in the position panel. Use these to manage risk and avoid liquidation.

Maintenance margin is the minimum amount required to keep a position open. It's based on the total size of your position rather than the leverage you select. As position size increases, higher portions fall into higher maintenance margin tiers, each with progressively higher rates.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin#liquidation)

**Liquidation**

If your margin falls below the maintenance requirement, your position may be liquidated to prevent further losses. Keep a close eye on your margin ratio and funding rates to stay safe.

[PreviousCosts of Opening Positionschevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/costs-of-opening-positions)
[NextCalculating Maximum Transfers in Cross and Isolated Marginchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/margin/calculating-maximum-transfers-in-cross-and-isolated-margin)

# Fees & Specs | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/shield-mode/fees-and-specs#trading-fee)

**Trading Fee**

To celebrate the launch of Perp Shield Mode, we're conducting a limited-time zero-fee event. Both opening and closing positions will incur no fees.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/shield-mode/fees-and-specs#profit-share)

**Profit Share**

Aster has implemented a profit-sharing model to reduce the impact of fees on users. When the position is profitable, a fee range from 15% to 20% will be charged on the profits. When the position incurs a loss, no fees will be incurred.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/shield-mode/fees-and-specs#flat-fee)

**Flat Fee**

A fixed fee rate applies to opening and closing positions. The current fee rate is 0.03%.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/shield-mode/fees-and-specs#dynamic-slippage)

**Dynamic Slippage**

The platform determines the slippage based on the liquidity of the pair's underlying assets and open interest, as observed from market performance.

# Shield Mode | Aster

**What is Shield Mode?**

Shield Mode offers a distinct trading experience compared to Order Book Futures, providing a quicker, easier, and more streamlined process. Users can trade faster and find it simpler to initiate their trades. Throughout the promotional period, there will be no opening or closing fees for trading transactions to reward our loyal Aster users.

# Auto Grid Trading | Aster

1.  Navigate to the right sidebar of the Futures Grid trading interface.
    
2.  On the \[Auto\] tab, review the recommended parameters and set your \[Initial Margin\].
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FKmCqWttJsjbvHYZA0z7O%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-15%252017.26.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7877ff5-9bb7-4e0d-85da-183a3e4231c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b3adf58&sv=2)

3\. Click \[Create\] and confirm your grid order. The system automatically places buy and sell orders at the preset prices.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FjMSpalWPHjBK2Dzt31E6%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-15%252017.27.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f5a659a-04b9-4165-b618-7c5d1c0b8027&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8647ba47&sv=2)

**Note:** The auto parameters function will not work if there is insufficient trading history for a given asset. In that case, set parameters manually or click \[Copy parameters to Manual settings\] to adjust the lower price, upper price, and grid number.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading#how-auto-parameters-are-calculated)

How Auto Parameters Are Calculated

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading#a398)

Upper & Lower Price (Bollinger Bands)

*   Upper Band = MA + bbm \* Standard Deviation
    
*   Lower Band = MA — bbm \* Standard Deviation
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading#id-5684)

Grid Number

Grid Number = (grid\_upper\_limit — grid\_lower\_limit)/ATR

\*Average True Range (ATR) for the past pre-defined hours of the selected symbol

**Risk Reminder:** Grid trading is a strategic tool and should not be considered financial or investment advice from Aster. If your grid settings are unreasonable, you may not capture grid revenue when the market moves in one direction outside your set range. Adjust your strategy based on current market conditions. Grid trading is used at your own discretion and risk. Aster is not liable for any losses arising from the use of this feature.

[PreviousManual Grid Tradingchevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/grid-trading/manual-grid-trading)
[NextLong/Short Grid Tradingchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/grid-trading/long-short-grid-trading)

# Fees | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/fees#fee-rates-for-usdt-perpetual-contracts)

**Fee Rates for USDT-Perpetual Contracts**

**Maker Fee:** 0%

A Maker order is one that adds liquidity to the order book. When you place a Maker order, you choose a price above or below the current market price, and your order is not filled immediately. Instead, it sits on the order book, waiting for another trader to match and fill it. You’re essentially making the market by placing an order that helps set available prices for others to trade.

**Taker Fee:** 0.04%

A Taker order is one that removes liquidity from the order book. When you place a Taker order, you’re trading immediately against an existing Maker order at the current available price. You're _taking_ liquidity by accepting someone else’s open order.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/fees#fee-rates-for-usd1-perpetual-contracts)

**Fee rates for USD1-Perpetual Contracts**

**Maker fee**: 0%

**Taker fee**: 0.005%

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/fees#pay-fees-with-usdaster-and-save-5)

**Pay Fees with $ASTER and Save 5%**

Save 5% on perp trading fees by paying with $ASTER. Simply deposit $ASTER into your perp wallet and it will automatically be used to cover fees. You can also transfer $ASTER from your spot account to your perpetual account to apply the discount.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/fees#how-fees-are-calculated)

**How Fees are Calculated**

In Aster Perps, transaction fees are based on the **nominal value** of your order — that is, the total value of the position you're opening or closing.

**Formula:**

*   **Transaction fee** = Nominal value × Fee rate
    
*   **Nominal value** = Number of contracts × Transaction price
    
    *   **Number of contracts**: Each contract typically represents a unit of the base asset — for example, 1 BTC in BTCUSDT contracts. So if you're trading 0.1 BTC, that’s 0.1 contracts.
        
    *   **Transaction price**: The price at which the trade happens (e.g. $80,000 for 1 BTC).
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/fees#example-1-market-buy-taker-order)

**Example 1: Market buy (Taker order)**

You place a **market order** to buy **0.1 BTC** at **$80,000**.

*   **Nominal value** = 0.1 × 80,000 = 8,000
    
*   **Transaction fee** = 8,000 × 0.04% = 3.20 **USDT**
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/fees#example-2-limit-sell-maker-order)

**Example 2: Limit sell (Maker order)**

Later, you place a **limit sell order** at **$85,000**.

*   **Nominal value** = 0.1 × 85,000 = 8,500
    
*   **Transaction fee** = 8,500 × 0 = **0 USDT**

# Stock Perpetuals | Aster

Aster perps supports **stock perps** — enabling perpetual futures trading for U.S. stocks, fully settled in USDT. Trade with up to 10x leverage, long or short, and choose your leverage level when placing an order.

Index prices are sourced from multiple providers including the Pyth oracle, ensuring a comprehensive and reliable data set for calculations and settlement.

The first stock listing is AAPL/USDT, offering a seamless, on-chain alternative for global traders to access equity markets with high flexibility and control.

Orders > 2% more aggressive than Mark Price will be rejected

Can fill up to 2% more aggressive than Mark Price; remainder is canceled

Market open

09:30–16:00

Same as crypto perpetual trading pairs

Same as crypto perpetual trading pairs

16:00–20:00

Orders > 2% more aggressive than Mark Price will be rejected

Can fill up to 2% more aggressive than Mark Price; remainder is canceled

Market close (off-hours)

20:00–04:00

Orders > 2% more aggressive than Mark Price will be rejected

Can fill up to 2% more aggressive than Mark Price; remainder is canceled

# Spot Fee Structure | Aster

In appreciation of our users' support, Aster is introducing a VIP program on Aster spot and Aster perpetual. Fees are based on your rolling 14 day volume and are assessed at the end of each day in UTC.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FbmRnvIqFiOOxwFavnCW1%252FAster%2520VIP%2520Program%2520Update.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03cf26f0-1b0a-4d5a-85f2-91b71639862e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad68edc5&sv=2)

**Maker fee**: 0.005%

Example: Buying 0.1 BTC at 100,000 with a maker order → 100,000 × 0.1 × 0.005% = 0.5 USDT

**Taker fee**: 0.04%

Example: Buying 0.1 BTC at 100,000 with a taker order → 100,000 × 0.1 × 0.04% = 4 USDT

The fee structure for current trading pairs, please visit our [Spot Trading arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/spot/CDLUSD1)
page.

**What are maker and taker?**

**Maker:** When you place an order with a set price and quantity that goes into the order book and waits to be filled, you are a maker. Maker orders add liquidity to the market.

**Taker:** When you place an order that matches and executes immediately against an existing order in the book, you are a taker. Taker orders remove liquidity from the market.

**How to use $ASTER to pay spot trading fees and get a 5% discount?**

You can save 5% on spot trading fees when you pay with $ASTER. Simply deposit $ASTER into your spot wallet, and toggle on 'Pay fee in ASTER'. As long as you have $ASTER in your spot wallet and settings toggled on, your $ASTER will be deducted to pay fees first with 5% discount.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FO4ave1hu4zg9CKA6sNpi%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-24%252011.07.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D990a9914-1561-4eea-835e-8577d4b1997d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7861736a&sv=2)

[NextOrder Typeschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/spot/order-types)

# Delistings | Aster

To maintain a healthy trading environment, Aster may delist certain perpetual futures contracts based on factors such as low liquidity or low trading volume. The delisting process is designed to be transparent and timely.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/delistings#reasons-for-delisting)

**Reasons for Delisting**

A futures contract may be delisted due to one or more of the following:

*   Low liquidity or trading volume
    
*   Project operations cease
    
*   Major changes to the underlying blockchain (e.g., a hard fork)
    
*   Other factors that negatively affect the trading experience
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/delistings#delisting-process)

**Delisting Process**

**Announcement**

A delisting notice will be issued on [Twitterarrow-up-right](https://twitter.com/asterdex)
, [Telegramarrow-up-right](https://t.me/asterdex)
, and [Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/asterdex)
 at least 24 hours in advance. The announcement will include the cessation of trading date and any relevant instructions.

**Reduce-Only Window**

Starting 10 minutes before the cessation of trading, only reduce-only orders can be placed for the affected contract. No new positions can be opened during this time.

**Final Mark Price Calculation**

During the last hour before trading stops, the Mark Price of the delisted contract is calculated as the average of the price index sampled every second — a total of 3,600 data points.

**Trading Halt and Settlement**

At the time of delisting:

*   All remaining open positions are automatically closed at the final Mark Price.
    
*   Trading fees are charged for the automatic settlement.
    
*   All unrealized PnL is settled and converted into realized PnL.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/delistings#after-delisting)

**After Delisting**

*   The delisted contract will no longer be available for trading.
    
*   Historical data may remain available for reference.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/delistings#recommendations)

**Recommendations**

To avoid automatic settlement and additional fees, traders are strongly advised to manually close all positions before the cessation of trading.

# Spot | Aster

Spot trading is a direct transaction between a buyer and a seller at the current market rate, known as the spot price.

For example, in the BTC/USDT pair, you can buy or sell 1 BTC at the spot price and pay or receive the equivalent amount in USDT.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/spot#whats-the-difference-between-spot-trading-and-perpetuals-trading)

**What’s the difference between spot trading and perpetuals trading?**

In spot trading, traders buy and sell the actual tokens of the underlying assets. For example, buying BTC in the spot market means you hold BTC in your account and benefit if its value increases.

In perpetuals trading, traders do not own the underlying asset. Instead, they trade perpetual contracts based on price movements. Perpetuals allow traders to go long when bullish or go short when bearish, without holding the actual token.

[NextDeposit & Withdrawal Guidechevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/spot/deposit-and-withdrawal-guide)

# Auto-Deleveraging (ADL) | Aster

Auto-Deleveraging (ADL) is a risk management mechanism that activates during extreme market conditions, used only when other protective systems – like liquidation and the insurance fund – cannot cover losses in time.

Auto-Deleveraging (ADL) is a risk management mechanism that activates during extreme market conditions, used only when other protective systems — like liquidation and the insurance fund — cannot cover losses in time.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/auto-deleveraging-adl#how-adl-works)

**How ADL Works**

When a position is liquidated but the execution price is worse than the bankruptcy price, the system absorbs the remaining loss. However, if the liquidation can't be completed before the Mark Price hits the bankruptcy price, ADL is triggered. This forcibly reduces the size of opposite-side positions held by other traders, starting with those who are most profitable and most highly leveraged.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/auto-deleveraging-adl#how-adl-priority-is-determined)

**How ADL Priority is Determined**

The system uses a ranking based on a trader's profit and leverage:

**Metric**

**Formula**

PnL percent

max(0, Unrealized profit) ÷ max(1, Wallet balance)

Margin ratio

If (Wallet balance + Unrealized profit) ≤ 0:

→ margin ratio = 0

If (Wallet balance + Unrealized profit) > 0:

→ Margin ratio = Maintenance margin ÷ (Wallet balance + Unrealized profit)

Leverage PnL

PnL percent × Margin ratio

Leverage PnL quantile

User's leverage PnL rank ÷ Total number of users

The higher your leverage PnL quantile, the higher your ADL risk.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/auto-deleveraging-adl#adl-risk-indicator)

**ADL Risk Indicator**

The LeveragePnLQuantile bar shows your risk of being auto-deleveraged:

*   4 bars = high ADL risk
    
*   Fewer bars = lower ADL risk
    

In Aster Pro, the LeveragePnLQuantile bar shows your risk of being auto-deleveraged:

*   4 bars = high ADL risk
    
*   Fewer bars = lower ADL risk
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FVUhltNkjAciejKmuGNav%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-01%252009.38.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91f523a9-1acc-4918-923d-d6a9ebd73cf9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4f4100b&sv=2)

This position is showing 1 of 4 bars - there is a low ADL risk

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/auto-deleveraging-adl#how-to-reduce-adl-risk)

**How to Reduce ADL Risk**

*   Lower your leverage
    
*   Close and reopen your position to reset your priority in the ADL queue
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/auto-deleveraging-adl#what-happens-if-youre-adld)

**What Happens If You're ADL'd**

Your position is partially or fully reduced without warning. You can re-enter the market at any time afterward.

Your position is partially or fully reduced without warning. You can re-enter the market at any time afterward.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/auto-deleveraging-adl#additional-notes)

Additional notes

*   The bankruptcy price might fall outside the current trading range, making it harder to fully close your position before losses exceed your margin
    
*   ADL mostly affects traders with high leverage and large unrealized profits
