# Order Types | Aster

[Aster Perpsarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
 supports several order types to give traders precise control over how and when their trades are executed.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FvpjHVBqEQq789QtzopND%252FOrder%2520panel.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D897d8063-6be4-4a9e-ae01-af60ac9efa41&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c15dd3c&sv=2)

Aster Pro's order tab

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#order-types)

**Order Types**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#id-1.-market-order)

**1\. Market Order**

A market order is an instruction to buy or sell immediately at the best available price. It prioritizes speed over exact price. Use market orders when you want to enter or exit a position quickly and are comfortable with potential slippage.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#id-2.-limit-order)

**2\. Limit Order**

A limit order lets you set the exact price at which you want to buy or sell. The order only executes if the market reaches your chosen price, giving you full price control.

**Example:** BTC is trading at 62,000 USDT. If you want to buy only if the price dips, you can place a limit buy at 61,800. The order will sit on the order book and only execute if the market reaches that level.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#id-3.-stop-limit-order)

**3\. Stop Limit Order**

A stop limit order combines two prices: a stop price and a limit price. When the stop price is reached, the system places a limit order at your specified limit price. This gives more control than a stop market order because execution is based on a limit price.

**Example:** You hold a long BTC position at 62,000 and want to protect against a drop. You set a stop price at 61,500 and a limit price at 61,480. If BTC falls to 61,500, a limit sell at 61,480 is placed. If the market falls too fast and never trades at 61,480, the order may remain unfilled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#id-4.-stop-market-order)

**4\. Stop Market Order**

A stop market order converts into a market order once the stop price is reached. It prioritizes guaranteed execution, though the final fill price may differ from the stop price due to market volatility.

**Example:** You're long BTC from 62,000 and want to cut losses if it breaks support. You set a stop market at 61,500. If BTC drops to 61,500, a market sell is triggered at the best available price — which may be 61,490 or 61,470 depending on conditions.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#id-5.-trailing-stop-order)

**5\. Trailing Stop order**

A trailing stop order sets a stop price that follows the market as it moves in your favor. If the price reverses by a set percentage, a market order is triggered. For more details, refer to : [Trailing Stop Orderarrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetuals/order-types/trailing-stop-order)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#id-6.-post-only-order)

**6\. Post Only Order**

A post only order ensures your limit order is added to the order book as a maker order. If your order would immediately match an existing order, it will be rejected. This is useful when you want to avoid taker fees.

**Example:** BTC is at 62,000. You place a post only limit sell at 62,001. If that price is already matched by a buyer, the platform rejects your order because it would execute immediately. If the best bid is 62,000, your order is posted as a maker order at 62,001.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#order-modifiers)

**Order modifiers**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#tp-sl-take-profit-stop-loss)

**TP/SL (Take Profit / Stop Loss)**

TP and SL let you set automatic exit levels when opening a position.

*   **Take Profit (TP):** Closes your position once the market reaches your target profit level, securing gains without manual monitoring.
    
*   **Stop Loss (SL):** Closes your position if the price moves against you, limiting losses and managing risk.
    

Aster gives you two price references for TP/SL:

*   **Mark price:** The fair price used for liquidation checks. TP/SL based on mark price tends to be more stable during volatility.
    
*   **Last price:** The latest traded price on the order book. TP/SL based on last price reacts more quickly but can be triggered by wicks or sudden spikes.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#reduce-only)

**Reduce Only**

A Reduce Only order guarantees that your order will never open or increase a position — it can only reduce or fully close an existing one.

Use this when:

*   You want to close part of a position without accidentally flipping direction.
    
*   You are setting TP or SL and want them to act as exits only.
    
*   You want to avoid accidentally adding to a position when intending to scale out.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#bbo-best-bid-offer)

**BBO (Best Bid/Offer)**

A BBO order places a limit order at the best bid or ask price. For a buy order, BBO sets the price at the lowest current ask; for a sell order, it sets the price at the highest bid.

If using Post Only mode, the order will only be placed if it adds liquidity. Due to market fluctuations, the order may fail to place if the market moves before it's confirmed.

Different BBO options such as \[Counterparty 1\] and \[Queue 1\] adjust the order price based on the market side and position (best or fifth-best price).

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#time-in-force-tif-options)

**Time-in-Force (TIF) Options**

Time-in-Force settings control how long your order remains active and under what conditions it should be canceled.

**GTC (Good Till Cancelled):** The order stays open until filled or manually canceled. Default for most limit orders.

**IOC (Immediate or Cancel):** Fills immediately at the available quantity; any unfilled portion is canceled.

Example: You place a limit order for 1 BTC and only 0.6 BTC is available at your price. The system fills 0.6 BTC and cancels the remaining 0.4 BTC.

**FOK (Fill or Kill):** The entire order must fill immediately; if it can't, the whole order is canceled.

Example: You place a limit order for 1 BTC and only 0.9 BTC is available. The entire order is canceled — nothing is filled.

[PreviousSingle-Asset Mode & Multi-Asset Modechevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/single-asset-mode-and-multi-asset-mode)
[NextHidden Orderchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types/hidden-order)

Last updated 25 days ago

*   [Order Types](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#order-types)
    
*   [Order modifiers](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#order-modifiers)
    
*   [Time-in-Force (TIF) Options](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/order-types#time-in-force-tif-options)

# Mint asBTC | Aster

asBTC is a liquid staking token for Bitcoin. Deposit BTC on Aster Earn to mint asBTC and earn yield through managed trading strategies, while retaining a liquid token you can withdraw at any time.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#key-benefits)

**Key Benefits**

*   Up to 5% APY, generated from trading strategies and reflected in asBTC's net asset value.
    

Assets are held with Ceffu, an institutional-grade third-party custodian, with audited smart contracts.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#how-to-mint-asbtc)

**How to Mint asBTC**

**Note:** Currently available on BNB Chain only.

1.  Go to Aster Earn and click **\[Connect Wallet\]**. Sign the message to connect.
    
2.  Select **BTC** from the dropdown menu.
    
3.  Click **\[Approve BTC\]**.
    
4.  Enter your desired BTC amount.
    
5.  Click **\[Mint asBTC\]** and confirm in your wallet.
    

Your asBTC will begin earning yield immediately.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#how-to-withdraw-asbtc)

**How to Withdraw asBTC**

1.  Go to Aster Earn and select **asBTC** from the dropdown.
    
2.  Enter your withdrawal amount.
    
3.  Click **\[Request Withdraw\]** and confirm.
    
4.  Withdrawals are processed within 14 days. Track status in the **\[Claim\]** section.
    
5.  Once processed, click **\[Claim\]** to receive your BTC.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#faqs)

**FAQs**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#what-is-asbtc)

**What is asBTC?**

A liquid staking token minted by depositing BTC on Aster Earn. Holding asBTC earns passive yield.

Contract address: `0x184b72289c0992BDf96751354680985a7C4825d6`

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#how-is-apy-generated)

**How is APY generated?**

Deposited BTC is deployed in stable trading strategies. Returns are distributed back to holders and reflected in asBTC's net asset value — your token value grows over time. Current APY is displayed on the Aster Earn page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#can-i-withdraw-at-any-time)

**Can I withdraw at any time?**

Yes, subject to a 14-day processing period.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#what-is-ceffu)

**What is Ceffu?**

An institutional digital asset custody platform. Ceffu holds deposited BTC using advanced security protocols and risk management controls.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#are-there-fees)

**Are there fees?**

No fees to mint or withdraw.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asbtc#what-are-the-risks)

**What are the risks?**

Smart contracts are fully audited and risk management protocols are in place. See the security documentation for details.

[NextMint asUSDFchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asusdf)

# Aster ALP | Aster

ALP is the liquidity pool token for Aster. Mint ALP to participate in onchain perp contract market-making and earn from platform trading activity.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp#how-alp-works)

**How ALP Works**

The ALP pool provides liquidity across all trading pairs on Aster perps. ALP holders act as the market-maker counterparty for perp trades on the platform.

ALP's net asset value (NAV) moves with the pool's overall profit and loss. This means ALP price can rise or fall depending on trading activity and market conditions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp#yield-sources)

**Yield Sources**

All yield is automatically reflected in ALP's NAV — your token value grows as the pool earns.

Source

Description

**Trading P&L**

ALP's share of market-making profit from Simple Mode trading activity.

**Trading Fees**

Protocol fees collected on trades.

**Funding Fees**

Fees from perpetual contract funding rate mechanisms.

**Liquidations**

Profit captured from liquidation events within the pool.

**Platform Fees**

Additional NAV boost from platform-level fee collection.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp#supported-networks)

**Supported Networks**

ALP can be minted on BNB Chain and Arbitrum. Supported deposit assets differ between chains — switch networks before minting to see available options.

[NextHow to Mint ALPchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/how-to-mint-alp)

# Sub Accounts | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#overview)

**Overview**

Sub-accounts allow you to run multiple independent trading strategies under a single master account. Each sub-account maintains its **own positions, assets, and API keys**, enabling effective risk isolation across different strategies.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-1.-requirements-and-limits)

**1\. Requirements & Limits**

**Item**

**Rule**

Minimum VIP level

VIP 2 or above, or MM accounts

Maximum sub-accounts

Up to 15 per master account

Sub-account nesting

Not supported

If your VIP level is below VIP 2, please upgrade before using the sub-account feature.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-2.-creating-a-sub-account)

**2\. Creating a Sub-Account**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#how-to)

**How to**

1.  Connect your **master account wallet** on Aster Web.
    
2.  Click your wallet address (top-right) → **Sub-account management** → **Create Sub-account.**
    
3.  Enter the sub-account name and configure trade settings (asset mode, position mode, etc.)
    
4.  Save your private key immediately. The system generates a wallet address and private key (EVM or Solana, matching your master account type). This key is shown only once and is never stored by Aster.
    
5.  Click Confirm and save, then confirm again in the second prompt. After closing the dialog, the key CANNOT be recovered.
    

Each sub-account creation requires a **wallet signature from the master account**.

Reminder: Aster never stores your private key. If you lose it, you cannot independently log in to or manage that sub-account. Save it to a secure location before dismissing the dialog.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#naming-rules)

**Naming Rules**

*   6 to 20 characters
    
*   Must include at least one letter
    
*   Numbers are allowed
    
*   Special characters are not supported
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-3.-account-switching)

**3\. Account Switching**

After creating sub-accounts, a dropdown menu will appear in the wallet panel.

*   First switch requires a wallet signature
    
*   Subsequent switches do not require re-signing (unless session is reset)
    

Important:

*   Switching is only available when logged in as the master account
    
*   When logged in directly as a sub-account, switching to other accounts is not supported
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-4.-fund-management)

**4\. Fund Management**

Sub-accounts support deposits and internal transfers, but not direct withdrawals.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#deposits)

**Deposits**

Sub-accounts support the same onchain deposit methods as the master account.

*   The system will remind you to confirm that you have saved your private key
    
*   Solana deposits directly to sub-accounts are not supported (Use internal transfers as an alternative for Solana)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#internal-transfers)

**Internal Transfers**

Internal transfers between master and sub-accounts are:

*   Instant
    
*   No fees
    

Supported transfer directions (when logged in as master):

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FZwQyHZNfKZm9Xru9C8WI%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49f908e4-688f-48c6-804f-b0ba4b597d07&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1e9bddc&sv=2)

**From**

**To**

**Allowed**

Master (Futures / Spot)

Own Sub-account (Futures / Spot)

Yes

Sub-account

Own Master (Futures / Spot)

Yes

Sub-account

Other sub-accounts under the same master account

Yes

Master account

Other Master accounts

Yes

Master account/Sub-account

Sub-accounts under a different master account

No

**Additional rules:**

*   Each transfer requires a wallet signature
    
*   Only assets with balance > 0 are displayed
    
*   Assets are sorted by value
    
*   Transferable amount equals withdrawable balance
    

When logged in directly as a sub-account, transfers are not available. To transfer funds, log in as the master account and switch to the target sub-account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#withdrawals)

**Withdrawals**

Sub-accounts cannot withdraw directly. To withdraw from sub-accounts, transfer funds to the master account, then withdraw from the master account.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-5.-feature-permissions)

**5\. Feature Permissions**

**Feature**

**Master Account**

**Sub-Account**

Futures & Spot trading

Yes

Yes

On-chain deposits

Yes

Yes

Withdrawals

Yes

No

Internal transfers

Yes (Unrestricted)

Not available (log in as master and switch to sub)

Create / manage sub-accounts

Yes

No

Account switching

Yes

No

API key limit

30

10

API withdrawal permission

Enabled

Permanently disabled

Referral binding between master & sub-accounts

No

No

Email login support

Yes

Not supported

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-6.-freezing-and-unfreezing-sub-accounts)

**6\. Freezing & Unfreezing Sub-Accounts**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#freeze-a-sub-account)

**Freeze a Sub-Account**

Go to Sub-account management → click \[⋯\] → Disable sub-account → click confirm

After freezing:

*   New positions are not allowed
    
*   Existing positions remain open, and will not be forced closed.
    
*   One-way mode: only reduce-only orders allowed
    
*   Hedge mode: only closing positions allowed
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#unfreeze-a-sub-account)

**Unfreeze a Sub-Account**

Go to Sub-account management → Click \[⋯\] → Enable sub-account to restore normal trading functionality.

Note: Deleting sub-accounts is not supported in the current version.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-7.-sub-account-api-keys)

**7\. Sub-Account API Keys**

*   Each sub-account can create up to 10 API keys (master account limit: 30)
    
*   Sub-accounts only support V3 API
    
*   Withdrawal permission is permanently disabled on all sub-account keys — calling the withdrawal endpoint returns a permission error.
    

To create a sub-account API key:

1.  Log in as the master account
    
2.  Switch to the target sub-account
    
3.  Create the API key (sub-account limit: 10)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-8.-vip-level-and-leaderboard)

**8\. VIP Level & Leaderboard**

*   VIP level is calculated based on combined data from the master account and all sub-accounts
    
*   The entire account group shares the same VIP tier and benefits
    
*   On the leaderboard, only the master account address is displayed
    
*   Sub-account trading volume is aggregated into the master account
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-9.-referrals-and-other-features)

**9\. Referrals & Other Features**

**Feature**

**Description**

Referral / rebates

Each account participates independently, rebates are calculated separately

Portfolio view

Each account sees its own assets (master aggregation is planned for future release)

USDF

Participated independently per account

Invitation relationships

Master and sub-accounts cannot refer to each other. Each account can establish its own referral relationship with an unrelated third party

Trades between master & sub-accounts

Counted as self-trading

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#id-10.-frequently-asked-questions)

**10\. Frequently Asked Questions**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#can-i-log-in-directly-with-a-sub-account)

**Can I log in directly with a sub-account?**

Yes. Use the sub-account's wallet address and private key to log in.

However, switching to master account or other sub-accounts is not supported within the same session.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#what-if-i-lose-the-sub-account-private-key)

**What if I lose the sub-account private key?**

It cannot be recovered. Aster does not store private keys. Always save your private key securely when creating the sub-account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#why-cant-i-create-a-sub-account)

**Why can't I create a sub-account?**

Sub-account creation requires VIP 2 or above. Please check your current VIP level.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#can-a-sub-account-create-its-own-sub-accounts)

**Can a sub-account create its own sub-accounts?**

No. Only the master account can create and manage sub-accounts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#can-email-login-accounts-use-sub-account-features)

**Can email login accounts use sub-account features?**

No. Sub-account functionality is only available for wallet-connected accounts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/sub-accounts#can-i-transfer-funds-to-another-sub-account-when-logged-in-as-a-sub-account)

**Can I transfer funds to another sub-account when logged in as a sub-account?**

No. When logged in directly as a sub-account, transfer functionality is not available. To transfer funds between accounts, log in as the master account and use the internal transfer function.

# Fund Custody & Risk Management | Aster

Aster partners with [Ceffuarrow-up-right](https://www.ceffu.com/)
 for the custody of USDF and underlying USDT funds, and to prepare funds for yield strategy execution on behalf of asUSDF holders.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#how-ceffu-ensures-safe-custody)

**How Ceffu Ensures Safe Custody**

Ceffu provides institutional-grade crypto asset management solutions with a focus on security and advanced technology. Their custody services include:

*   Cold storage for offline asset protection
    
*   Off-exchange settlement to reduce counterparty exposure
    
*   Multi-party computation (MPC) and multi-signature wallets for distributed key management
    
*   Private key encryption secured in hardware devices or cryptographic vaults
    
*   Custom governance controls and institutional-grade security measures
    

Ceffu's solutions meet rigorous institutional standards and compliance requirements, making them a trusted custodian for digital assets.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#mirrorx-capital-deployment-with-security)

**MirrorX: Capital Deployment with Security**

Ceffu's MirrorX solution is key to generating staked USDF (asUSDF) yields. MirrorX allows Aster to deploy capital on Binance instantly while keeping assets in Ceffu's independent custody.

**How it works:**

*   Maintains a 1:1 balance delegation from Ceffu to a Binance sub-account
    
*   Assets always remain in Ceffu's custody (not on Binance)
    
*   Trades settle off-exchange, minimizing counterparty risk
    
*   Withdrawals settle on T+1 basis
    

This structure combines deep exchange liquidity with institutional-grade security. The Aster-Ceffu account executes the delta-neutral strategy by buying spot assets on Binance while shorting corresponding perpetual contracts to maintain balanced positions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#audit)

Audit

Before deploying any asset, Aster conducts rigorous evaluation to assess market fit and potential risks. All smart contracts are audited by reputable security firms, and Aster maintains a robust risk monitoring system.

**USDF Audit report**

[Audit Reportschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/overview/audit-reports)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#risk-factors)

**Risk Factors**

Understanding potential risks helps you make informed decisions. USDF faces both general stablecoin risks and those specific to yield-bearing assets.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#smart-contract-risk)

**Smart Contract Risk**

**What it is:** The potential for malicious actors to exploit loopholes in smart contracts.

**Mitigation:** Aster engages reputable security firms for audits and maintains robust risk monitoring. Aster works with security and blockchain partners to stay current with the latest DeFi security developments and liaises regularly with risk monitoring teams.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#underlying-asset-risk)

**Underlying Asset Risk**

**What it is:** USDT, which backs USDF, carries its own risks–most notably the possibility of depeg and reserve backing concerns.

**Mitigation:** You can review current USDT balances, reports, and reserves at [Tether's transparency dashboardarrow-up-right](https://tether.to/en/transparency/?tab=usdt)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#custodial-partner-risk)

**Custodial Partner Risk**

**What it is:** Potential failure of operations at Ceffu, such as accessibility issues, inability to process transactions, or failure to settle positions regularly. There's also risk if Ceffu fails compliance, security, or data privacy standards.

**Mitigation:** Ceffu holds [ISO 27001 and 27701 certificationsarrow-up-right](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/ceffus-solution-receives-iso-27001-and-iso-27701-certification)
 and is [SOC 2 Type 1 & 2 compliantarrow-up-right](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/upholding-trust-and-safety-ceffu-renews-soc-2-attestation)
, meaning auditors have independently verified their cybersecurity and privacy controls. [Ceffu is also part of the Global Travel Rule (GTR) Alliancearrow-up-right](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/ceffu_joins_global-travel_rule_alliance_digital_asset_compliance)
 to comply with FATF Recommendation 16. Aster actively monitors for custodial partner risks and is prepared to react quickly if issues arise.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#exchange-partner-risk)

**Exchange Partner Risk**

**What it is:** If Binance becomes insolvent, delta-neutral positions would become ineffective, impacting yield generation.

**Mitigation:** Aster proactively monitors exchange partner status and is prepared to respond quickly to any issues.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#funding-risk)

**Funding Risk**

**What it is:** Perpetual shorts in the delta-neutral strategy earn funding fees. Consistently negative funding rates require the Aster account to pay more fees, reducing asUSDF APY.

**How it works:** Funding rates fluctuate, especially during market volatility. While negative rates directly reduce APY, perpetual markets are designed to balance long and short open interest. Negative funding rates typically return to a positive mean over time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#liquidation-risk)

**Liquidation Risk**

**What it is:** When perpetual positions exist, sudden large price movements could trigger automatic liquidations if collateral falls below margin requirements.

**Mitigation:** The Aster account on Ceffu regularly monitors positions and frequently settles profit/loss to keep liquidation risk minimal.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdf-stablecoin/overview/fund-custody-and-risk-management#prospects-and-future-growth)

**Prospects & Future Growth**

During market downturns, USDF offers a reliable option for steady returns. Staking USDF for asUSDF unlocks an additional yield opportunity from the previously described delta-neutral strategies.

Aster sees significant market potential for expanding yield sources. Future opportunities include:

*   Integration of real-world assets (RWAs) like US Treasury Bonds
    
*   New arbitrage strategies and on-chain mechanisms
    
*   Enhanced capital efficiency and yield generation
    

Aster's commitment is to provide safe, productive investment options even during challenging economic conditions.

# Team Boosts | Aster

Every referral family forms a team. Teams earn a points multiplier based on their combined hourly trading activity — the more your team trades, the higher the boost applied to everyone's points.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/aster-convergence-stage-6/team-boosts#who-is-on-your-team)

Who Is on Your Team

A team consists of up to four tiers within your referral chain:

Member

Role

**A**

The person who invited you

**B**

Other people invited by A

**C**

You

**D**

People you invited

**Example:** Yuki invited you and Wyn. You invited Zen, who invited Ben.

*   Your team: Yuki (A), Wyn (B), you (C), Zen (D)
    
*   Ben is not on your team — he's a second-level referral (referral of your referral).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/aster-convergence-stage-6/team-boosts#how-it-works)

**How It Works**

Team boost is calculated from the team's combined points across Spot and Perpetual trading. In Stage 6, boosts accumulate continuously throughout the entire campaign — unlike Stage 2 where they reset each epoch. Your team's progress is never lost.

When a new member joins, the boost takes effect within a few hours — no need to wait for the next epoch.

**Example:** Wyn (600k), Yuki (300k), and Zen (100k) earn 1,000,000 team points in an hour, qualifying for a 1.05× boost:

*   Wyn: 600,000 → 630,000
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 → 315,000
    
*   Zen: 100,000 → 105,000
    

Team Points (hourly snapshot)

Boost

3,000,000

1.05×

15,000,000

1.10×

45,000,000

1.15×

90,000,000

1.20×

# Pre-Launch Contracts | Aster

Pre-launch contracts or pre-markets allow users to trade token pairs before they are officially listed on major exchanges. They are structured as expiry futures contracts, but may also take the form of perpetual futures. Once the token launches and begins trading, the pre-market symbol on Aster Perps converts to a regular perp futures contract.

Aster has the right to initiate the delivery process automatically when a token launches on an external exchange or when the token's tokenomics are released. Pre-market mode will switch to a perpetual contract automatically.

**Aster retains final authority over the delivery price and the right to delist the contract.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/pre-launch-contracts#mark-price-pre-launch-usdt-margined-futures-contracts)

**Mark Price (Pre-Launch USDT-Margined Futures Contracts)**

Aster uses the Mark Price to avoid unnecessary liquidations and to prevent market manipulation. The Price Index for pre-launch markets is calculated differently from regular perpetual futures.

**The Mark Price formula:**

(1) Mark Price = Median × (Price 1 , Price 2 , Contract Price)

(2) Price 1 = ( Bid 1 + Ask 1) / 2 × (1 + Funding Rate × (Time to Next Funding Rate (h)/8 ))

(3) Price 2 = ( Bid 1 + Ask 1) / 2

_Bid 1 & Ask 1 are sourced from the pre-market order book._

_The median is the middle value of Price 1, Price 2, and the Contract Price. For example, if Price 1 < Price 2 < Contract Price, then Price 2 is taken as the Mark Price._

_Price 2 logic may be updated based on market conditions._

Once the pre-market symbol transitions to a regular perpetual futures contract, the index price calculation also switches to the standard perpetual futures methodology.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/pre-launch-contracts#related-docs)

# Privacy Policy | Aster

This Privacy Notice (“Notice”) describes how Aster (“Aster”, “we”, “us”, “our”, “ourselves”) collects and processes your Personal Data (“you”, “your”) through our websites ([https://www.asterdex.comarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/)
) and applications or other services (collectively, together with our websites and apps, our “Services”). In addition, we may also process your Personal Data for specific purposes, where applicable, such as processing your job applications or administering your employment with us. By using our Services or engaging with us, you consent to the collection, storage, processing, and transfer of your Personal Data as described in this Privacy Notice.

This Privacy Notice applies together with our Terms of Use, any terms of business or other contractual documents, including but not limited to any agreements we may have with you.

**This Notice covers:**

[1\. Our Relationship with You](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-1.-our-relationship-with-you)

[2\. Collection and Use of Your Personal Data](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-2.-collection-and-use-of-your-personal-data)

[3\. How and Why We Share Your Data](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-3.-how-and-why-we-share-your-data)

[4\. International Transfer of Personal Data](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-4.-international-transfer-of-personal-data)

[5\. Data Security](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-5.-data-security)

[6\. Data Retention](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-6.-data-retention)

[7\. What Privacy Rights Do You Have?](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-7.-what-privacy-rights-do-you-have-your-privacy-rights)

[8\. Children](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-8.-children)

[9\. Contact Information](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-9.-contact-information)

[10\. Conditions of Use, Notices and Revisions](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-10.-conditions-of-use-notices-and-revisions)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-1.-our-relationship-with-you)

1\. Our Relationship with You

Your right to privacy and the protection of your Personal Data is important to us. Aster is committed to the best practices in privacy, and we will only collect data when it’s strictly necessary to provide our Services.

By using Aster’s Services, including, for example, visiting our website, using our application, interacting on social media or community forum, participating in our offline events (and this list is not exhaustive), you acknowledge and accept the use, disclosure, and procedures outlined in this Privacy Notice.

Aster is the data controller responsible for processing your information. If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or our data practices, please contact us through our [online formarrow-up-right](https://submit-irm.trustarc.eu/services/validation/4ceeff02-b44a-4cdb-bb95-3a43b2db026d/?brandId=98b1bece-4e60-4ce6-ae54-07e9168e6eda)
. The following sections provide further details as to how we process your Personal Data through Aster as the Data Controller.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-2.-collection-and-use-of-your-personal-data)

2\. Collection and Use of Your Personal Data

“Personal Data” is information that may identify an individual or relates to an identifiable individual. This includes information you provide voluntarily to us, information which is collected or created automatically in the natural course of provision of our Services, or otherwise when you contact us. Following best practices in privacy such as data minimisation, we endeavour to collect only the amount of Personal Data that is necessary to provide our Services to our users.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#when-you-use-our-services)

When You Use Our Services

You can browse our websites without creating an account. However, if you choose to access our Services, we will need to collect certain personal details to provide and manage your use of those Services.

Below, we present a list that outlines the Personal Data that the Services use and the purposes for processing that information.

*   Wallet Information: This may include your wallet ID, public wallet address, and transaction details. We use this information to facilitate, execute, and manage the transactions you request.
    
*   Profile or Contact Information: This may include your Name, email address. authenticate and manage user accounts if you choose to.
    
*   Social Media information: This may include details you choose to share during your interaction with us via channels such as X, Google, or other social login services. We use this information to enable the authentication and login to our Services, interact with you in our community, enable participation in events or campaigns, and keep you updated on announcements.
    
*   Business Contact Information: This may include your Name, email address, Telegram handle, company, country. We use this information to process and respond your enquiries or handling of business communication.
    

We primarily rely on the legal basis of contract performance to process your Personal Data in connection with your use of our Services. For certain optional features, we may also rely on your consent or our legitimate interests, as appropriate.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#connect-using-third-party-social-login-platforms)

Connect Using Third-Party Social Login Platforms

We offer you a seamless connection to our Services through third-party platforms, such as Wallet Connect or other Social Login such as Google, X etc. You can easily access our Services using your existing wallet or login from these platforms. By using or continuing to use your third-party account to log in, you acknowledge that we may receive certain information (such as your wallet address or profile information) from that platform as needed to enable your connection. Please note that these third-party platforms are independent of us, and their processing of your Personal Data is subject to their own privacy notices. We process the Personal Data obtained through social login features (such as your account identifier and basic profile information) on the legal basis of performance of a contract, as this processing is necessary to provide you with access to and use of our Services.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#recruitment-and-employment)

Recruitment and Employment

If you apply for a position with us or become employed by us, we collect and process your Personal Data for purposes including recruitment, onboarding, employment administration, compliance with legal obligations, and other employment-related activities. Personal Data may be collected directly from you, from third-party recruitment agencies, or from publicly available sources such as LinkedIn.

We process the following categories of Personal Data for recruitment and employment purposes:

*   Contact Information: We will collect your name, email address, and other relevant contact details to communicate with you about your job application and, where applicable, your employment.
    
*   Education and Employment Information: We collect your Curriculum Vitae (CV), resume, LinkedIn profile, academic certificates and transcripts, employment history, and (where relevant) salary and bonus details. We use this information to assess your suitability, process your application, conduct background checks, and manage your employment relationship.
    

During recruitment, we rely on your consent to process your Personal Data. Once employed, we rely on the necessity to perform your contract, comply with legal obligations, and our legitimate interests in managing the employment relationship.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#ambassador-program)

Ambassador Program

When you voluntarily apply to or participate in our Ambassador Program, we collect and process your Personal Data to assess your application and to administer and manage your participation in the program. The Personal Data is collected directly from you.

We process the following categories of Personal Data for purposes set out below:

*   **Contact Information:** This may include your name, email address, and relevant contact details (such as social media handles). We use this information to communicate with you regarding your application, onboarding, and ongoing participation in the Ambassador Program.
    
*   **Digital Wallet information:** This may include your public wallet address(es) and country of residence. We use this information to facilitate the distribution of any rewards or benefits associated with the program and to comply with applicable legal and regulatory requirements. We do not collect or process your private keys.
    

During application, we rely on your consent to process your Personal Data. Once you are accepted into the program, we rely on the necessity to perform your contract, comply with legal obligations, and our legitimate interests in managing the volunteering relationship.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#personal-data-collected-automatically-from-you)

Personal Data collected automatically from you:

In certain circumstances, we may collect Personal Data automatically from you when you use our Services, in accordance with applicable laws. This may include device, log, and usage data, which helps us enhance your experience, provide customer support, improve the performance of our sites and Services, and safeguard your account by detecting unauthorized access and preventing fraud.

Log and Usage Data. When you access or use our Services, our servers automatically collect service-related, diagnostic, usage, and performance data, which is recorded in log files. This log data may include your IP address, device information, browser type, settings, and details about your activity within the Services (such as timestamps, pages and files viewed, searches performed, and features used). It may also include device event data like system activity, error reports (such as "crash dumps"), and hardware settings.

Our legal basis for processing this log and usage data is our legitimate interest in improving our Services, ensuring the security of our Services, and maintaining a safe environment for our users, including fraud monitoring and prevention.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#aggregated-and-anonymized-data)

Aggregated and Anonymized Data

We also use aggregated or anonymized data to improve our Services. This involves analyzing general usage trends, gathering feedback, and conducting research without identifying individual users. For example, we may create overall usage reports for specific regions without containing Personal Data.

We will not use your Personal Data for purposes that are incompatible with the purposes of which you have been informed, unless it is required or authorized by law, or it is in your own vital interest to do so.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-3.-how-and-why-we-share-your-data)

3\. How and Why We Share Your Data

Information about our users is an important part of our business and we are not in the business of selling our user’s Personal Data to others. We may transfer Personal Data to our service providers or third parties in connection with Aster’s operation of its business, as certain features on Aster rely on various third-party products and services (collectively “Third Party Services”), such as processing of web hosting, cloud storage, analytics, and improvement of website-related services and features, and performance of maintenance services.

Third Party Services providers must only process the Personal Data in accordance with our contractual agreements and only as permitted by applicable data protection laws.

We may also share Personal Data with the following persons or in the following circumstances:

*   **Affiliates:** Personal Data that we process and collect may be transferred between companies, Services, and employees affiliated with us (collectively, our “Affiliates”) as a normal part of conducting business and offering our Services.
    
*   **Business Transfers:** As we continue to develop our business, we might sell or buy other businesses or services. In such transactions, user information generally is one of the transferred business assets but remains subject to the promises made in any pre-existing Privacy Notice (unless, of course, the user consents otherwise). Also, in the unlikely event that Aster or substantially all of its assets are acquired, users' information will be one of the transferred assets.
    
*   **Legal Authorities:** We may be required by law or by Court to disclose certain information which might cover Personal Data or any engagement we may have to relevant regulatory, law enforcement and/or other competent authorities. We will disclose Personal Data to legal authorities to the extent we are obliged to do so according to the law. We may also need to disclose Personal Data in order to enforce or apply our legal rights or to prevent fraud.
    
*   **Protection of Us and Others:** We will share Personal Data outside of Aster if we have a reasonable belief that access, use, preservation, or disclosure of the information is reasonably necessary to comply with any applicable law, regulation, legal process, or enforceable governmental request; to cooperate with law enforcement; to enforce or apply our Terms of Use and other agreements; or to protect the rights, property, or safety of Aster, our employees, our users, or others. This includes exchanging information with other companies and organizations for fraud protection and credit risk reduction, and with regulatory agencies and law enforcement to comply with lawful requests.
    

Our Services and websites may contain links that enable you to connect with various third-party websites, applications, and other external platforms (referred to as "Third Party Platforms"). These Third Party Platforms act as independent data controllers and their processing of your Personal Data will be subject to their privacy notices and policies. This Privacy Notice does not cover the privacy practices of these Third Party Platforms. A link to a third-party site does not imply endorsement by us or our Affiliates. Your use of these Third Party Platforms and their handling of your Personal Data will be governed by their respective terms and privacy policies, and not by this Privacy Notice.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-4.-international-transfer-of-personal-data)

4\. International Transfer of Personal Data

We maintain servers hosted by our trusted service providers, and your information may be processed on servers located outside of your country of residence. Additionally, we may transfer your Personal Data to our Affiliates, third-party partners, and service providers located in various countries around the world.

In instances where we process your Personal Data on servers outside your country or transfer it to third countries or international organizations beyond your country of residence, we implement appropriate technical, organizational, and contractual safeguards to ensure that your Personal Data remains protected. This includes, but is not limited to, the use of Standard Contractual Clauses. These measures ensure that any such transfers comply with applicable data protection laws and maintain an adequate level of protection for your Personal Data as outlined in this Notice.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-5.-data-security)

5\. Data Security

We recognize that information security is a crucial component of data privacy. We are committed to making sure your information is protected in accordance with applicable laws and our data privacy policies. Although no data transmission, including over the Internet or through any website, can be guaranteed to be entirely secure, we employ a range of commercially reasonable physical, technical, and procedural measures to protect Personal Data from unauthorized access, use, disclosure, alteration, or destruction.

The information you provide to us is stored on secure servers managed by us or our trusted service providers. Access to and use of this information are governed by our internal security policies and standards, or those agreed upon with our service providers, all in alignment with industry best practices.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-6.-data-retention)

6\. Data Retention

We keep your Personal Data to enable your continued use of our Services, for as long as it is required in order to fulfill the relevant purposes described in this Privacy Notice as may be required by law such as for tax and accounting purposes, or to resolve disputes and/or legal claims or as otherwise communicated to you.

When we have no ongoing legitimate business or legal requirement to retain your Personal Data, we will either delete or anonymise such information, or, if this is not possible (for example, because your Personal Data has been stored in backup archives), then we will securely store your Personal Data and isolate it from any further processing until deletion is possible.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-7.-what-privacy-rights-do-you-have-your-privacy-rights)

7\. What Privacy Rights Do You Have? Your Privacy Rights

Subject to applicable laws, as outlined below, you have a number of rights in relation to your privacy and the protection of your Personal Data. These rights may be limited in some situations - for example, where we can demonstrate we have a legal requirement to process your Personal Data.

*   Right to access: You have the right to obtain a copy of the Personal Data that we hold about you as well as certain information related to its processing.
    
*   Right to correct: You can request the rectification of inaccurate Personal Data and and you may also provide additional information to complete your records. You can also change your Personal Data in your account at any time.
    
*   Request to erase your Personal Data: You may request the erasure of your Personal Data, including where such Personal Data would no longer be necessary to achieve the purposes for which it was collected. Please note that Personal Data may still need to be retained for compliance with applicable legal obligations.
    
*   Right to object: You can object, for reasons relating to your situation, to the processing of your Personal Data. For instance, you have the right to object where we rely on legitimate interest or where we process your data for direct marketing purposes.
    
*   Right to restrict processing: You have the right, in certain cases, to temporarily restrict the processing of your Personal Data by us, provided there are valid grounds for doing so. We may continue to process your Personal Data if it is necessary for the defense of legal claims, or for any other exceptions permitted by applicable laws.
    
*   Right to withdraw or opt out your consent: You have the right to withdraw your consent and request us to stop collecting, using and/or disclosing your Personal Data for any or all of the purposes listed above at any time. Exercising this right does not affect the lawfulness of the processing based on the consent given before the withdrawal of the latter.
    
*   Right to portability: You can also request us to provide your information in a structured way so you can send it to another service provider.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#submit-privacy-request)

Submit Privacy Request

Alternatively, to exercise your rights, you can submit a request using our [online formarrow-up-right](https://submit-irm.trustarc.eu/services/validation/4ceeff02-b44a-4cdb-bb95-3a43b2db026d/?brandId=98b1bece-4e60-4ce6-ae54-07e9168e6eda)
.

We will respond as quickly as possible. If we are unable to respond within 30 days, we will inform you in writing of the timeline for our response. If we cannot fulfill your request, we will explain the reasons (unless prohibited by applicable laws).

If you have any questions or concerns about how we collect and process your Personal Data, or if you wish to withdraw your consent for any processing, please contact us.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-8.-children)

8\. Children

We do not knowingly solicit data from or market to any persons under 18 years of age. By using the Services, you represent that you are at least 18 years old. If we become aware that we have collected Personal Data from someone under 18, we will deactivate the account in question and take reasonable measures to promptly delete all such data from our records unless we are legally required to keep it. If you become aware that any Personal Data we may have collected is from a user under the age of 18, please contact us using the contact information below.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-9.-contact-information)

9\. Contact Information

Our support team is available to direct any questions related to your Personal Data. You can contact us through our [online formarrow-up-right](https://submit-irm.trustarc.eu/services/validation/4ceeff02-b44a-4cdb-bb95-3a43b2db026d/?brandId=98b1bece-4e60-4ce6-ae54-07e9168e6eda)
, and we will ensure your inquiry reaches the appropriate team to address any concerns regarding the collection and processing of your Personal Data.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/resources/privacy-policy#id-10.-conditions-of-use-notices-and-revisions)

10\. Conditions of Use, Notices and Revisions

If you choose to use our Services, your use and any dispute over privacy is subject to this Privacy Notice and our Terms of Use. If you have any concerns about privacy at Aster, please contact us and we will try our best to resolve it. You also have the right to contact your local Data Protection Authority.

We reserve the right to update and revise this Notice at any time. We will review this Privacy Notice from time to time to make sure it complies with applicable laws and conforms to changes in our business. If we do revise this Privacy Notice, we will update the “Last Updated” date at the beginning of this Notice so that you can tell if it has changed since your last visit and will do our best to notify you.

Please review this Privacy Notice regularly to ensure that you are aware of its terms. Your continued use of our Services after an amendment to our Privacy Notice constitutes your acceptance to the amended terms.

# Grid Trading | Aster

Grid trading lets you automate strategies and capture market swings without constant monitoring. By placing buy and sell orders at preset price intervals, you can profit from volatility whether the market is moving up, down, or sideways.

Aster supports three grid strategies: neutral, long, and short — giving you the flexibility to match your approach to different market conditions. You can use auto-generated parameters or configure your own.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/grid-trading#in-this-section)

In this section

*   [**Set up your grid strategy**arrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-pro/grid-trading/set-up-your-grid-trading-strategy)
    
*   [**Auto grid trading guide**arrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-pro/grid-trading/futures-grid-trading-auto-parameters-guide)
    
*   [**Long/short grid trading**arrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-pro/grid-trading/long-short-grid-trading-introduction)

# How to Burn ALP | Aster

1.  Go to [https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/alparrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/alp)
    . Check that you are on the correct network (you can only mint and burn ALP on BNB Chain and Arbitrum networks).
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FBtnudeJCWbOJK2yjf9Gz%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.39.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De390c3ea-f38f-47ac-807a-758d0279a9cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=69d9e001&sv=2)

1.  After connecting your wallet, click **\[Burn ALP\]**.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FKZdVt1fUBUrOgXWNPFf5%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.52.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1aab4229-1079-4746-b3e1-85a42b486ef2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c5a8a4e&sv=2)

**Notes:**

*   ALP cannot be burned within 48 hours of minting.
    
*   The maximum amount you can burn at any time is capped based on available pool liquidity:
    
    **Max burnable ALP = (Pool value − Your position value) × 50% ÷ ALP market price**
    
    **Example:** Pool value is 10,000,000 USDT, your position value is 5,000,000 USDT, ALP price is 2 USDT → maximum burnable = 1,250,000 ALP.
    
*   Upon burning, assets received cannot exceed what's available in the pool. If a specific asset (e.g. USDT) has insufficient balance to cover your full redemption, the remainder can be burned for other assets held in the ALP pool.
    

[PreviousHow to Mint ALPchevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/how-to-mint-alp)
[NextALP Feeschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees)

Last updated 20 days ago

# Human vs AI: Battle for the futures $200,000 Reward Pool | Aster

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fq7n6IzuaOu93zZ80URa5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35b335ea-d4ce-4293-9644-f31b3ba26868&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86c6207b&sv=2)

[**Human vs AI: The Ultimate Trading Battle**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/campaigns/human-vs-ai)

**$200,000 Prize pool. 100 funded traders. Zero downside. Team Human vs AI.**

For decades, humans dominated trading. Intuition. Experience. The ability to read what data fails to capture.

Then came the AI models. GPT-5. Gemini. Deepseek. Grok and more. Running 24/7, processing millions of signals in seconds, executing without fear.

Now it’s time to let **Team Human** and **Team AI** settle this on-chain.

* * *

**The Most Asymmetric Bet in Crypto**

Aster is funding **up to 100 human traders** with **10,000 USDT each** to fight the world’s leading AI models in a live, real-size Perpetual competition.

If you are selected:

*   You keep every dollar of profit
    
*   Aster absorbs every dollar of loss
    

On top of that, you’re not just trading for yourself. You’re playing for **Team Human.**

*   Total prize pool: $200,000
    
*   $100,000 for the top Human PnL champion
    
    *   Prize goes unclaimed if AI takes #1.
        
    
*   Human team base prize pool: $50,000.
    
    *   If humans beat AI, the prize pool DOUBLES to $100,000.
        
    *   Every profitable human trader shares the prize pool.
        
    

Apply now to represent Team Human: [Register Nowarrow-up-right](https://forms.gle/yrKzPgMHZ8ynMkVF6)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#usd200-000-prize-pool-overview)

$200,000 Prize Pool Overview

1.  **Individual Prize**
    
    *   Top PnL Champion: $100,000
        
    *   The $100,000 prize is awarded only if the top PnL trader is Human.
        
    *   If an AI trader takes the #1 PnL spot, this individual prize is not awarded.
        
    
2.  **Human Team Prizes**
    
    *   Base Prize: $50,000
        
    *   If **Team Human** beats **Team AI**, the Human Team prize pool **doubles to $100,000**.
        
    *   Human team rewards are distributed **proportionally based on each trader’s positive PnL** (human champion excluded).
        
    *   **Reward for each eligible Human trader** = (Individual Positive PnL ÷ Total Positive PnL of all eligible Human team members) × Human Team Prize Pool.
        
    
    Notes:
    
    1.  PNL calculation: PNL = Total balance (including unrealized PNL + wallet balance) - Initial Trading Funds
        
    2.  Team ROI = Sum of all team members’ PNL / Total Initial Trading Funds of all team members
        
    3.  Only traders with positive PNL (PNL > 0) are eligible to share the team rewards. Rewards are distributed strictly according to each trader’s share of total **positive** Human team PNL.
        
    4.  **Rewards are paid in USDF**, Aster’s yield-bearing stablecoin.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#key-dates)

Key Dates

*   Sign-up period: from now to 23:59 UTC, 4 Dec
    
*   Eligible participant announcement: 7 Dec.
    
    *   Eligible participants will be notified individually via X direct messages.
        
    *   Please keep DMs open and monitor messages from @Aster\_DEX
        
    
*   Trading competition: 12:00 UTC, 9 Dec - 23:59 UTC, 23 Dec
    
*   Reward distribution: Before Jan 14, 2026.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#participants)

Participants

*   The competition is open to up to 100 selected traders.
    
*   Participants will be chosen based on historical performance, including trading volume and PnL over the past 60 days.
    
*   Team AI unites cutting-edge models from the world’s leading AI research labs, featuring GPT, Gemini, DeepSeek, Grok, and more.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#competition-funds-house-money-only)

Competition Funds: House Money Only

*   Each participant receives 10,000 USDT in a dedicated competition account before the competition begins.
    
*   No external funds or additional capital may be added.
    
*   All losses are fully covered by Aster, and negative balances do not require repayment.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#account-restrictions)

Account Restrictions

1.  Once eligibility is confirmed, Aster will create a dedicated competition account for each participant and credit it with 10,000 USDT before the event begins.
    

*   Deposits, withdrawals, and transfers are immediately disabled.
    
*   These restrictions remain active throughout the pre-event period and the entire event.
    

1.  Please note that after the event concludes, Aster will gradually close all remaining open positions for users who have not closed them.
    
2.  After the competition ends, all participants must immediately stop trading and refrain from performing any actions on their accounts. Any post-event activity, including opening or closing positions, modifying orders, or transferring funds, will be considered a violation and will result in forfeiture of all prizes and eligible profits.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#competition-rules)

Competition Rules

*   Only Perpetuals Futures trading volume will be counted.
    
*   Only USDT-margined trading is eligible for the competition.
    
*   If two participants achieve identical PNL, the trader with the higher valid trading volume ranks higher.
    
*   All activities in this competition are excluded from Stage 4: Harvest and any other ongoing campaigns or reward programs on the Aster platform.
    
*   Participation implies agreement with Aster’s Terms & Conditions.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#ai-model-protocol-and-operating-rules)

AI Model Protocol & Operating Rules

All the trades that are executed live with real funds, and models must rely solely on prompt-based decision-making without any form of prior training, fine-tuning, or external data feeds.

1.  **Standard LLMs only** Eligible models include, but are not limited to, GPT-5, GPT-4, Gemini 3, DeepSeek V3.1, Grok 4, QWEN 3 Max, Claude Sonnet 4/4.5, ERNIE Bot, KIMI, and other widely available, non-fine-tuned LLMs. Custom models, proprietary fine-tuning, or specialized trading versions are strictly prohibited.
    
2.  **Prompt-only control** All trading logic must be controlled exclusively through prompts. No code execution, no multi-agent frameworks, no custom toolchains.
    
3.  **Live trading with real funds.** There is no simulated data at any stage. All orders are executed on live markets with real funds. This ensures:
    

*   Real slippage
    
*   Real funding rates
    
*   Real volatility exposure
    
*   Real execution latency
    

1.  **No fine-tuning or training.** Every prompt execution must occur fresh. Participants are forbidden from:
    

*   Training models on historical trading data
    
*   Uploading reinforcement-learning results
    
*   Using custom LoRA, SFT, or RLHF variants
    
*   Updating or re-prompting based on prior trading logs
    

1.  **No conversation memory.** Every inference must operate in a clean, memory-isolated environment. Models do not receive:
    

*   Previous trades
    
*   PnL history
    
*   Their own prior outputs
    

1.  **No external information** such as news, sentiment, or off-platform data feeds. Models cannot access:
    

*   Live news
    
*   Social media sentiment (X, Telegram, Reddit, etc.)
    
*   On-chain signals
    
*   Proprietary feeds
    
*   Any real-time market data beyond what is explicitly provided in the standardized prompt
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#reward-distribution)

Reward Distribution

*   The public leaderboard will be updated periodically and provides provisional rankings only.
    
*   After the event ends, Aster will conduct a full audit of all participant accounts to verify trading behavior, rule compliance, and data accuracy. The official final rankings will be announced separately once the review is complete.
    
*   After the audit, Aster will distribute the rewards (Final balance - the initial 10,000 USDT + the prize amount) to the participant’s personal Aster Spot account provided during registration.
    
*   The ‘Final balance’ will be determined based on the snapshot taken at the end of the competition. Any profits generated from trades executed after the competition ends will not be counted, and any remaining USDT will be reclaimed by Aster.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/program-and-rewards/points-and-campaigns/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#terms-and-conditions)

Terms & Conditions

*   Fraudulent or manipulative trading activity (e.g. wash trading) will result in disqualification.
    
*   Aster may amend or modify campaign rules at any time without prior notice.
    
*   Aster retains the final right of interpretation for this event.
    
*   Aster will not be responsible or liable for any losses (including, without limitation, any direct or indirect damages for loss of profits) resulting or arising directly or indirectly from your participation in this campaign.
    
*   Any fraudulent, manipulative, or abusive trading activity (including but not limited to wash trading) will result in disqualification and forfeiture of rewards and trading profits.
    
*   Aster may amend, modify, or terminate campaign rules at any time without prior notice, if required to protect market integrity or user interests.
    
*   Aster retains the final right of interpretation for this event and its outcomes.
    
*   Aster will not be responsible or liable for any losses (including, without limitation, direct or indirect losses or loss of profits) arising directly or indirectly from participation in this campaign.

# How to Mint ALP | Aster

    . Check that you are on the correct network (you can only mint ALP on BNB Chain and Arbitrum networks).
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FAouy5Iuzembuh1sgrI99%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.39.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D342ae6b1-4d55-4e9f-96fa-2ab1bcc21b39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0d24a5f&sv=2)

# Direct Contract Interaction | Aster

Some users choose to interact directly with the contract for full control, automation, or when the app interface is unavailable or limited.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/1001x/direct-contract-interaction#how-to-get-trading-pair-information)

How to Get Trading Pair Information

*   **Contract address**: 0x1b6f2d3844c6ae7d56ceb3c3643b9060ba28feb0
    
*   **Method**: ParisV3
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/1001x/direct-contract-interaction#response)

**Response:**

Copy

      struct LeverageMargin {
            uint256 notionalUsd;
            uint16 tier;
            uint16 maxLeverage;
            uint16 initialLostP; // 1e4
            uint16 liqLostP;     // 1e4
        }
    
        struct SlippageConfig {
            string name;
            uint256 onePercentDepthAboveUsd;
            uint256 onePercentDepthBelowUsd;
            uint16 slippageLongP;       // 1e4
            uint16 slippageShortP;      // 1e4
            uint16 index;
            ISlippageManager.SlippageType slippageType;
            bool enable;
        }
    
        struct FeeConfig {
            string name;
            uint16 index;
            uint16 openFeeP;     // 1e4
            uint16 closeFeeP;    // 1e4
            bool enable;
            uint24 shareP;       // 1e5
            uint24 minCloseFeeP; // 1e5
        }
    
        struct PairView {
            // BTC/USD
            string name;
            // BTC address
            address base;
            uint16 basePosition;
            PairType pairType;
            PairStatus status;
            uint256 maxLongOiUsd;
            uint256 maxShortOiUsd;
            uint256 fundingFeePerBlockP;  // 1e18
            uint256 minFundingFeeR;       // 1e18
            uint256 maxFundingFeeR;       // 1e18
    
            LibPairsManager.LeverageMargin[] leverageMargins;
    
            uint16 slippageConfigIndex;
            uint16 slippagePosition;
            LibPairsManager.SlippageConfig slippageConfig;
    
            uint16 feeConfigIndex;
            uint16 feePosition;
            LibFeeManager.FeeConfig feeConfig;
    
            uint40 longHoldingFeeRate;    // 1e12
            uint40 shortHoldingFeeRate;   // 1e12
      }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/1001x/direct-contract-interaction#id-1.-how-to-open-a-position-at-the-opening-price)

**How to open a position at the opening price**

*   **Contract address:** 0x1b6f2d3844c6ae7d56ceb3c3643b9060ba28feb0
    
*   **Method**: openMarketTrade
    
*   **Parameters**: data (tuple) Tuple: A tuple is an array of values e.g. \[ "0x4sd…","100","100"..\]. It can contain strings, integers, and boolean values. The structure for this tuple is:
    

**Example**: If the user wants to use 100 USDT to place a pending order for a BTC Long position with Price 20000, Quantity 0.001, Take Profit Price 25000, and Stop Poss price 19000, the inPutData should be:\["0x7130d2a12b9bcbfae4f2634d864a1ee1ce3ead9c","True","0x55d398326f99059fF775485246999027B3197955","100000000000000000000","10000000",,"2000000000000"2500000000000","1900000000000",1\]

            // Pair.base

            bool isLong;
            // BUSD/USDT address

            uint256 amountIn;   // tokenIn decimals

            // Market Trade: worst price acceptable
            uint256 price;      // 1e8
            uint256 stopLoss;   // 1e8
            uint256 takeProfit; // 1e8
            uint256 broker;
        }

            // Pair.base

            uint256 price;      // 1e8
            uint256 stopLoss;   // 1e8
            uint256 takeProfit; // 1e8
            uint256 broker;
        }

# ALP Fees | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#mint-and-burn-fees)

**Mint and Burn Fees**

To encourage a balanced pool composition, mint and burn fees adjust dynamically based on how far each asset's current weight deviates from its target weight. Depositing an underweight asset lowers your fee; depositing an overweight asset raises it.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#fee-parameters-usdt-current-values)

Fee Parameters (USDT current values)

Parameter

Description

Current Value

**FeeBasisPoints**

Base fee rate

0.25%

**TaxBasisPoints**

Adjustment rate applied based on weight deviation

0.05%

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#mint-fee-calculation)

**Mint Fee Calculation**

1.  **Current asset value:** `InitialValue = AssetValueInPool + AssetUnrealizedPnL`
    
2.  **Asset value after minting:** `AfterMintValue = InitialValue + MintValue`
    
3.  **Target asset value:** `TargetValue = (TotalPoolValue + TotalUnrealizedPnL) × TargetWeight`
    
4.  **Weight deviation before minting:** `InitialDiff = InitialValue − TargetValue`
    
5.  **Weight deviation after minting:** `AfterDiff = AfterMintValue − TargetValue`
    

Condition

Formula

`AfterDiff < InitialDiff` (minting moves asset closer to target)

`MintFee = Max(FeeBasisPoints − TaxBasisPoints × InitialDiff / TargetValue, 0)`

`AfterDiff ≥ InitialDiff` (minting moves asset further from target)

`MintFee = FeeBasisPoints + TaxBasisPoints × Min((InitialDiff + AfterDiff) / 2, TargetValue) / TargetValue`

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#burn-fee-calculation)

**Burn Fee Calculation**

1.  **Current asset value:** `InitialValue = AssetValueInPool + AssetUnrealizedPnL`
    
2.  **Asset value after burning:** `AfterBurnValue = InitialValue − BurnValue`
    
3.  **Target asset value:** `TargetValue = TotalPoolValue × TargetWeight`
    
4.  **Weight deviation before burning:** `InitialDiff = InitialValue − TargetValue`
    
5.  **Weight deviation after burning:** `AfterDiff = AfterBurnValue − TargetValue`
    

Condition

Formula

`AfterDiff < InitialDiff` (burning moves asset closer to target)

`BurnFee = Max(FeeBasisPoints − TaxBasisPoints × InitialDiff / TargetValue, 0)`

`AfterDiff ≥ InitialDiff` (burning moves asset further from target)

`BurnFee = FeeBasisPoints + TaxBasisPoints × Min((InitialDiff + AfterDiff) / 2, TargetValue) / TargetValue`

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#example)

**Example**

Pool value: $10,000,000 | Unrealised PnL: +$10,000 | BTC in pool: $1,000

BTC target weight: 2% | Current weight: 0.01% | FeeBasisPoints: 0.25% | TaxBasisPoints: 0.45%

Since BTC is significantly underweight, minting ALP with 1 BTC incurs a **0% fee**. Burning ALP to receive 1 BTC (removing an already scarce asset) incurs a **0.7% fee** (0.007 BTC).

You can view the current pool composition, asset quantities, values, and target vs. current weights directly on the ALP page. After selecting an asset and quantity, the interface will display the exact fee before you confirm the transaction.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FVVnuNsPUi14hf3Yk4hsx%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252013.56.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df45faaaf-582f-4430-9991-387a6313d16e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2bcb68f0&sv=2)

[PreviousHow to Burn ALPchevron-left](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/how-to-burn-alp)
[NextEcosystemchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem)

Last updated 22 days ago

*   [Mint and Burn Fees](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#mint-and-burn-fees)
    
*   [Mint Fee Calculation](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/aster-alp/alp-fees#mint-fee-calculation)

# Aster API | Aster

The Aster API lets you connect your account programmatically and manage operations securely using API keys.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/for-developers/aster-api#id-1.-create-an-api-key)

**1\. Create an API Key**

Generate an API key from your account settings. During setup you can configure IP whitelisting and set permissions — read access, write access, or both.

→ [How to Create an API Keyarrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/api/how-to-create-api)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/for-developers/aster-api#id-2.-explore-the-api-documentation)

**2\. Explore the API Documentation**

Once you have an API key, you can begin making authenticated requests. The API documentation includes request formats, parameters, and response examples.

→ [View API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/api/api-document)
