        "f":"GTC",					// Time in Force\
        "q":"0.001",				// Original Quantity\
        "p":"0",					// Original Price\
        "ap":"0",					// Average Price\
        "sp":"7103.04",				// Stop Price. Please ignore with TRAILING_STOP_MARKET order\
        "x":"NEW",					// Execution Type\
        "X":"NEW",					// Order Status\
        "i":8886774,				// Order Id\
        "l":"0",					// Order Last Filled Quantity\
        "z":"0",					// Order Filled Accumulated Quantity\
        "L":"0",					// Last Filled Price\
        "N":"USDT",            	// Commission Asset, will not push if no commission\
        "n":"0",               	// Commission, will not push if no commission\
        "T":1568879465651,			// Order Trade Time\
        "t":0,			        	// Trade Id\
        "b":"0",			    	// Bids Notional\
        "a":"9.91",					// Ask Notional\
        "m":false,					// Is this trade the maker side?\
        "R":false,					// Is this reduce only\
        "wt":"CONTRACT_PRICE", 		// Stop Price Working Type\
        "ot":"TRAILING_STOP_MARKET",	// Original Order Type\
        "ps":"LONG",						// Position Side\
        "cp":false,						// If Close-All, pushed with conditional order\
        "AP":"7476.89",				// Activation Price, only puhed with TRAILING_STOP_MARKET order\
        "cr":"5.0",					// Callback Rate, only puhed with TRAILING_STOP_MARKET order\
        "rp":"0"							// Realized Profit of the trade\
      }\
      \
    }\
\
Copy\
\
    {\
        "e":"ACCOUNT_CONFIG_UPDATE",       // Event Type\
        "E":1611646737479,		           // Event Time\
        "T":1611646737476,		           // Transaction Time\
        "ac":{								\
        "s":"BTCUSDT",					   // symbol\
        "l":25						       // leverage\
         \
        }\
    }  \
     \
\
Copy\
\
    {\
        "e":"ACCOUNT_CONFIG_UPDATE",       // Event Type\
        "E":1611646737479,		           // Event Time\
        "T":1611646737476,		           // Transaction Time\
        "ai":{							   // User's Account Configuration\
        "j":true						   // Multi-Assets Mode\
        }\
    }  \
\
Copy\
\
    {\
      "code":-1121,\
      "msg":"Invalid symbol."\
    }

# asUSDF on Pendle | Aster

asUSDF is the yield-bearing token of USDF. Staking USDF on Aster mints asUSDF, which earns yield from the delta-neutral positions backing USDF — reflected in asUSDF's net asset value.

Read more about asUSDF and USDF:

[Mint asUSDFchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/mint-asusdf)

On Pendle, asUSDF can be split into its principal and yield components, giving you three ways to engage depending on your goal.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#lp-asusdf-provide-liquidity)

**LP-asUSDF — Provide Liquidity**

Deposit asUSDF as liquidity on Pendle to receive LP-asUSDF. LP positions earn yield from four sources: underlying yield from USDF, PT fixed yield, $PENDLE incentives, and Pendle swap fees.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F1z51GAEQpXGstIFIi5CC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4111e4e6-2ddd-4716-aafe-b6ab291cfb91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=302d093e&sv=2)

Adding asUSDF liquidity

**Note:** Pendle labels underlying yield as coming from USDF because USDF is the underlying stablecoin of asUSDF.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcfFSR4v5q9eIWdxF4s4TCnNhmOqhxeJDunkBas_AXl0x93LfCXzulGxNY0m1QzRqr2ANDRV4L_-q4oO4sefatSKn5bXRychNYp0jRcR9d-k2oCxDSQREhrwXuE2PMXcCP5mGoztQ%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a21995d&sv=2)

LP-asUSDF Yield

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#pt-asusdf-fixed-yield)

**PT-asUSDF — Fixed Yield**

PT-asUSDF represents the principal portion of asUSDF, traded at a discount. At maturity, 1 PT-asUSDF redeems for 1 asUSDF at a 1:1 ratio.

Buying PT-asUSDF locks in a fixed APY for the period — the discount you buy in at becomes your guaranteed return if held to maturity.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfWP7ArNfWRthwNgA7uljBgrdUJUHrM1JsvzXFXbTXNzJFNKwno9tykQ-0e7sV3CB7cwnNziVOu7eA5ccc17gI2g51OsnH0J5gv56uQoWwlBMUWk1KcQqgRrLOdD3DG4cQKAUIr%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b315ac3&sv=2)

Buying PT-asUSDF

**Example:** PT-asUSDF offering 18.39% fixed APY maturing 29 May 2025 returns 18.39% APY if held to maturity, regardless of asUSDF's underlying yield performance.

*   You do **not** earn asUSDF underlying yield as a PT holder.
    
*   You can hold to maturity or trade PT-asUSDF on Pendle at any time.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#yt-asusdf-yield-exposure)

**YT-asUSDF — Yield Exposure**

YT-asUSDF represents the yield portion of asUSDF. Holding 1 YT-asUSDF gives you the yield that would accrue on 1 asUSDF until maturity.

This is a leveraged yield position — you pay a fraction of asUSDF's value to capture all its yield output. YT-asUSDF trends toward $0 as maturity approaches, since remaining yield decreases over time. You profit if the total yield collected exceeds what you paid for the YT.

You can hold to maturity or trade YT-asUSDF on Pendle at any time.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcVCFbHD_Qz8S3hoGI7upzsykLNn26OkmsSemXdyaQYNFJfplWiJHItZq7cxOyRTgsdU6caKgxbtns7mGwS5c-iyEZDwNSnmkQqeEyb_5UtNnpFTGb5-TpS_n0xSEBAWDw2kpj4%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe5d3043&sv=2)

Buying YT-asUSDF

Last updated 22 days ago

# LP on PancakeSwap | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**arrow-up-right](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

**Page Summary**

[1\. Mint & Hold asToken StableSwap LPs](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#id-1.-mint-and-hold-astoken-stableswap-lps)

[2\. Stake StableSwap LPs](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#c05a)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#id-1.-mint-and-hold-astoken-stableswap-lps)

1\. Mint & Hold asToken StableSwap LPs


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Earn Au points for minting & holding [**StableSwap LP**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)
 **tokens**.

*   **If you mint V3 LP tokens, you do not get Au points.**
    
*   **Minting StableSwap LP is NOT the same as LP staking.**
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fu9r8XjE4zgXb2G9I0dTz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d5dbf52-ddd5-4d5c-8b9d-9d0670c29be9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfc010c0&sv=2)

*   USDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 35x Au
    
*   asUSDF/USDF StableSwap LP: 30x Au
    
*   asUSDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 25x Au
    
*   asCAKE/CAKE StableSwap LP: 2x Au
    

**How is Au calculated?**

Au points are accrued based on the USD value of the StableSwap LP tokens minted. For example, if you add liquidity to the asUSDF/USDT stable LP on PancakeSwap, which has a 25x Au multiplier, and minted 20 USD worth of stable LP tokens, you should get 20 x 25 = 500 Au. You will continue earning 500 Au/hour.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#c05a)

2\. Stake StableSwap LPs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Please note that LP Staking is NOT the same as minting & holding** [**StableSwap LPs**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)
**. LP Staking is only available for the following StableSwap pairs:**

*   USDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 35x Au + APR
    
*   asUSDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 25x Au + APR
    

**How do I stake my StableSwap LP?**

Please connect your wallet to PancakeSwap and go to \[My Positions\]. If you already hold StableSwap LPs, click \[Stake LP\] and confirm.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FUTCxjGjjcyaHzeRWwOO6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9bda713-081b-4ed5-a8c9-7107deb21989&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a5ceec4&sv=2)

**How is Au calculated?**

Au multiplier for staking a StableSwap LP is the same as the multiplier for minting and holding. For example, minting and holding asUSDF/USDT stable LP has a 25x Au multiplier. Staking asUSDF/USDT stable LP thus also has a 25x Au multiplier.

Scenario:

*   If you have 20 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP and staked all of it, you continue earning 20 x 25 = 500 Au/hour.
    
*   If you stake 10 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP and continue holding 10 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP, you will earn 10 x 25 = 250 Au/hour from staking and 10 x 25 = 250 Au/hour from holding.
    

**What does APR consist of?**

When you stake StableSwap LPs on PancakeSwap, you also earn Combined APR in the form of CAKE tokens. Combined APR consists of Farm APR and LP fee APR. Please read this for more details about Farm APR: [https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/yield-farmingarrow-up-right](https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/yield-farming)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FMQOVMQCcaSvGufc8sGRH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6e0cc3d-75df-42af-af00-b876b2640643&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7e5b5bf&sv=2)

**How do I collect CAKE token rewards?**

Go to your staked positions and click \[Harvest\] to collect CAKE rewards.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FYeN7pXcf7t2e1mmqJbKO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6000a0b-2966-4f04-9de4-6713234361bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=545bad27&sv=2)

# Mark price | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#overview)

**Overview**

On [Aster Proarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
, the **mark price** serves as a reference price to calculate traders' unrealized profit and loss (PnL). It helps reduce unnecessary forced [liquidationsarrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/liquidations)
 during periods of abnormal market volatility, ensuring fair and accurate pricing of perpetual contracts.​

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#price-index)

**Price index**

The **price index** is a weighted average derived from major spot markets such as Binance, Huobi, and Kraken. Markets with higher trading volumes have a greater influence on the index value. This index represents the fair value of the asset's spot price and is used to calculate the mark price, which is crucial for determining unrealized PnL.​

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#mark-price-calculation)

**Mark price calculation**

The mark price is determined by taking the median of three prices:​

*   **Price 1**: Price index × (1 + Funding rate × (Time to next funding rate in hours ÷ 8))
    
*   **Price 2**: Price index + 5-minute moving average
    
*   **Contract Price**: The current contract price​
    

The **5-minute moving average** is calculated by sampling every minute over a 5-minute interval:​

Moving average = Average of ((bid 1 + ask 1) ÷ 2 − Price index)​

The **mark price** is the median of Price 1, Price 2, and the Contract Price. For example, if Price 1 < Price 2 < Contract Price, then Price 2 is selected as the Mark Price.​

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#handling-abnormal-market-conditions)

**Handling abnormal market conditions**

In cases of significant deviations between price sources or abnormal market conditions causing large differences between the spot price and the mark price, Aster Pro may implement precautionary measures:​

*   **Single price source deviation**: If the last price from a particular exchange deviates more than 5% from the median price of all sources, that exchange's price weight is set to zero.
    
*   **Multiple price source deviations**: If more than one exchange shows a deviation greater than 5%, the median price of all sources is used as the index value instead of the weighted average.
    
*   **Exchange connectivity issues:** If any exchange fails to update its price feed within 3 seconds, that source is removed from the price index calculation. This prevents outdated prices from influencing the mark price.
    
*   **Last trade price protection:** If the latest trade price deviates more than 5% from the mark price and no new trade occurs within 5 seconds, the contract price is replaced with the current mark price in the mark price calculation. This prevents the system from using stale or potentially manipulated trade prices in liquidation-related processes.
    

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Overview](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#overview)
    
*   [Price index](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#price-index)
    
*   [Mark price calculation](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#mark-price-calculation)
    
*   [Handling abnormal market conditions](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/mark-price-1#handling-abnormal-market-conditions)

# Liquidations | Aster

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#understanding-liquidation-mechanics)

Understanding liquidation mechanics

In [Aster Proarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
, liquidations are designed to protect both traders and the platform during periods of high volatility. Aster uses both the **last price** and the [**mark price**arrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/mark-price)
 to manage liquidation processes effectively:

*   **Last price**: This is the most recent transaction price of a contract and is used to calculate realized profit and loss (PnL).​
    
*   **Mark price**: Calculated based on a combination of funding data and a basket of prices from multiple spot exchanges, the mark price is used to determine unrealized PnL and trigger liquidations.​
    

Risk and leverage are adjusted based on exposure; larger positions require higher margin and offer lower leverage.​

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#when-liquidation-occurs)

When liquidation occurs

A forced liquidation is triggered when:​

**Margin = Initial Collateral + Realized PnL + Unrealized PnL < Maintenance margin**​

To avoid liquidation (i.e., when the risk ratio hits 100%), it's recommended to maintain a margin ratio below 80% by adding sufficient margin or reducing the position size.​

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#forced-liquidation-price)

Forced liquidation price

Forced liquidation occurs when the mark price reaches the liquidation price. Monitoring both the mark price and your liquidation price is crucial to prevent unwanted liquidations.​

In **cross margin** mode with hedge trading, both long and short positions of the same contract share the same liquidation price. In **isolated margin** mode, long and short positions have different liquidation prices based on the margin allocated to each.​

A built-in future calculator to compute liquidation prices is coming soon.​

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#forced-liquidation-process)

Forced liquidation process

When your margin falls below the maintenance requirement, the system initiates forced liquidation to limit further losses and protect the platform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#what-happens-during-liquidation)

What happens during liquidation:

*   All open orders on your account are immediately canceled.
    
*   A single large [**Immediate-or-Cancel (IOC)** orderarrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/order-types#time-in-force-tif-options)
     is submitted to reduce your position size. The system attempts to fill as much as possible and cancel the rest.
    
*   If your margin is sufficient after this step—accounting for realized losses and liquidation fees—liquidation stops.
    
*   If not, your remaining position is closed at the **bankruptcy price**, and the position is handed over to the **insurance fund**. Your account is then marked as **bankrupt**.
    

If your wallet balance becomes negative at this point, the insurance fund covers the loss and pays any outstanding fees. Any remaining assets (if applicable) are also allocated to the insurance fund.

Additional notes:

*   Different liquidation protocols may apply depending on your position’s size and risk level, helping to minimize the chance of full liquidation.
    
*   It’s advisable to close positions manually before approaching the maintenance margin threshold to avoid forced liquidation fees.
    
*   Smaller positions are generally more likely to be fully liquidated, as they have less margin buffer and may not qualify for partial liquidation. Larger positions benefit from margin tiering, which allows for more gradual risk reduction.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#liquidation-settlement-and-negative-balance-handling)

Liquidation settlement and negative balance handling

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#automatic-negative-balance-settlement)

Automatic negative balance settlement

If your account ends up with a **negative balance after liquidation**, Aster may use funds from the **insurance fund** to cover the loss — but only under specific conditions.

To qualify for **automatic settlement**, all of the following must apply:

*   The negative balance is in a **USDT perpetuals** account.
    
*   The account has **no open positions** (cross or isolated margin).
    
*   The negative balance is **no greater than 5,000 USDT**.
    
*   **No funds have been transferred** into the account after liquidation to offset the loss.
    

If you meet these conditions, the settlement will be handled automatically. If not, please contact us via [Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/invite/asterdefi)
 for further assistance.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#liquidation-settlement-fee)

Liquidation settlement fee

When your position is liquidated, a portion of the **liquidation fee** is allocated to the insurance fund. This appears in your transaction history as an **“Insurance Clearance Fee”**.

You can find more details on fee tiers in the Trading Rules page.

Additional notes:

*   Bankruptcy prices may fall outside the contract’s current market range.
    
*   Due to latency or syncing issues, some numerical values may update without notice.
    

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Understanding liquidation mechanics](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#understanding-liquidation-mechanics)
    
*   [When liquidation occurs](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#when-liquidation-occurs)
    
*   [Forced liquidation price](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#forced-liquidation-price)
    
*   [Forced liquidation process](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals/fees-and-specs/liquidations#forced-liquidation-process)

# Au Trader Boost | Aster

**Page Summary:**

[Au Trader Boost](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#b.-au-trader-boost-tiers)

[C. Au Points Calculation](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#c.-au-points-calculation)

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#a.-what-is-au-trader-boost)

A. What is Au Trader Boost?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recap: Au = Airdrop points you earn by minting and holding eligible assets. Rh = Airdrop points you earn by trading perps on Aster Pro mode.

**Au Trader Boost** is an incentive to encourage minters to trade on Aster Pro mode. Aside from earning Rh points, you may get an Au Trader Boost for your asset holdings if you hit certain trading volume criteria!

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#b.-au-trader-boost-tiers-new-adjustment-on-21-may)

B. Au Trader Boost Tiers (New adjustment on 21 May)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Total Trading Vol on Aster Pro in a day

Au Trader Boost (Adjust on 12 May)

New adjustment on 21 May

≥ 10k

2x

+1x

≥ 50k

2.4x

+2x

≥ 200k

2.6x

+2.5x

≥ 500k

3x

+3x

To calculate your Pro mode trading volume, use this formula: **Pro taker volume + (Pro maker volume\*0.5)**

For example, Alice conducted trades on Aster Pro on Monday, reaching a total trading volume of 50k. On Tuesday 00:00 UTC+0, the system calculates Alice's Pro mode trading volume and verifies that it corresponds to an Au Trader Boost of 2x. This boost will be reflected in Alice's airdrop dashboard and Alice receives an additional 2x boost on her Au points at 00:05 UTC+0 on Tuesday.

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#c.-au-points-calculation)

C. Au Points Calculation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The formula for calculating Au points is:

**Au = SUM( holding\_token\_USD\_value \* token\_AU\_multiplier ) \* (team boost + Trader boost) + ref bonus**

*   **Au** is the total airdrop points you get from minting and holding assets
    
*   **holding\_token\_USD\_value** refers to the USD investment of your underlying asset. For example, if you stake 0.5 BNB when BNB price is $670, your holding\_token\_USD\_value is 0.5 x 670.
    
*   **token\_AU\_multiplier** is the Au multiplier of the asset. For example, asBNB has a 5x Au multiplier.
    
*   **team boost** is the boost leverage of your team.
    
*   **Trader Boost** is the additional Au boost you earn from trading on Aster Pro mode.
    
*   **ref bonus** is the total Au points you have earned from your Tier 1 and 2 referrals.
    

Check your Au Trader Boost on the airdrop dashboard:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F3XKi4rjOzpsZYx4QonOq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6815f177-179b-4f06-bd43-f6fc462ee141&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b2cca67&sv=2)

# Trade like a Pro, Earn like a Pro | Aster

**Important Notice:**

*   The Stage 1 Rh Points Program has ended with Epoch 21 on June 22, 2025, 23:59 UTC+0, and distribution of Stage 1 Rh points has stopped. Stage 2 incentives will be announced in due time. [Read morearrow-up-right](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1935669044600082686)
    . _Last updated: June 23, 2025_
    

* * *

**Page Summary:** [1\. Why Pro Mode?](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-1.-why-pro-mode)
 [2\. Rh Points Calculation](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-2.-rh-points-calculation)
 [3\. FAQ](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-3.-faq)
 [4\. Terms & Conditions](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-4.-terms-and-conditions)

In the **Trade like a Pro, Earn like a Pro** program, earn Rh points in each Aster Stage 1 weekly epoch when you trade perpetuals on Aster Pro Mode. Refer friends, form teams and boost Rh!

Currently, **there is no fixed $ASTER token allocation percentage for each weekly epoch** in the Trade Like a Pro, Earn like a Pro program**.** This is termed 'blind mining' and each epoch's allocation will be determined at Aster's discretion.

*   Only trades on Aster Pro Mode via the Aster website earn Rh points.
    
*   You may qualify for extra rewards: 1.1x Rh points boost AND/OR 100 BonusUSD trading bonus. Remember to claim them before trading.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-1.-why-pro-mode)

1\. Why Pro Mode?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pro mode introduces an advanced order book interface with deep liquidity, up to 100x leverage and advanced trading tools. It doesn’t just provide a CEX-like experience; Pro mode’s fees are even lower than CEXs!

*   Fees: Maker 0.01%, Taker 0.035%
    
*   Multi-assets mode: Trade perps using different cryptocurrency assets as collateral
    
*   Referral program: 20% commission, with a tiered system in the works
    
*   Airdrop points: Trading on Pro mode earn you Rh points for the upcoming $AST airdrop
    

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-2.-rh-points-calculation)

2\. Rh Points Calculation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An epoch lasts one week, from Monday 00:00 UTC+0 to Sunday 23:59 UTC+0. Only the first epoch differs: Wednesday, 10 Apr. to Sunday, 13 Apr. 23:59 UTC+0.

Only trades on Aster Pro mode via the Aster website earn Rh points. Trades on Aster Simple mode (on-chain trading) and Dumb Mode do not earn Rh points. Your Rh balance updates every hour.

**Formula: Rh = \[Pro taker\_vol + (Pro maker\_vol\*0.5)\]\*(team boost + user\_Rh\_boost) + ref bonus**

For example:

*   If Alice’s taker\_vol is $100, maker\_vol is $200, and Alice has no team boost, Alice’s Rh = \[100 + (200\*0.5)\] = 200 Rh
    
*   If Alice’s taker\_vol is $100, maker\_vol is $200, and Alice has a team boost of 1.1x, Alice’s Rh = \[100 + (200\*0.5)\]\*(1.1) = 220 Rh
    

Note: Each trading pair has a minimum trading order size. Depending on the leverage selected, you will need a corresponding minimum principal. Please choose your leverage accordingly.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdIlC-HmJnFOM138P9gkEm_UkOVhAE56QZM1yUyxNhEUY_5jS_9vwaS0t-6xu6gMGZRXwtvP0xdC8NNK93lGd6pwHPdBtlWa8tSnmVsOWOaqJazjADgfgoVQ78kaGBQkBcIPzBQ%3Fkey%3Dxma8o7QrK4dbPiaixZMZQ3rV&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d587328&sv=2)

Your airdrop allocation from Rh points is determined by your Rh weightage in each epoch: **Your Rh weightage = sum(your total Rh in this epoch / all Rh in this epoch)**

Trade on Aster Pro Mode: [arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/BTCUSD)

[![Logo](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic.asterdexstatic.com%2Fcloud-futures%2Fstatic%2Fimages%2Fdex%2Faster%2Faster-favicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5292686c&sv=2)Aster - The next-gen perp DEX for all tradersAsterdexchevron-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)

Pro Trading Tutorial:

[Perpetualschevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading/perpetuals)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-3.-faq)

3\. FAQ


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What are Au points?**

Au points are Aster airdrop points for minting and holding eligible assets. Enjoy up to 20x Au multiplier when you mint and hold asTokens, USDF, ALP and eligible LP tokens. To see individual asset multipliers, please refer to [https://www.asterdex.com/en/earnarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
.

Your USD asset value is verified hourly and Au points stack hourly. For example, if you earned 100 Au points in the first hour, you would have 2400 Au points after 24 hours. Check your Au balance on the Aster airdrop dashboard.

**What are Rh points?**

Rh points are Aster airdrop points for trading on Aster Pro mode (Aster Simple mode and Dumb mode do not earn Rh points). To calculate your Rh points for each trade, refer to section 2. Rh Points Calculation.

Your Pro mode trading volume is verified hourly. However, unlike Au points, Rh points do not stack hourly. Check your Rh balance on the Aster airdrop dashboard.

**How can I boost my Au and Rh points?**

Boost your airdrop points when your friends bind your invite code before their first mint or trade. By forming a team, you and your friends can earn up to 1.2x points boost.

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-4.-terms-and-conditions)

4\. Terms & Conditions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Market makers cannot earn Rh points.
    
*   After the end of each epoch, Aster may adjust Trade like a Pro, Earn like a Pro (the 'Activity') rules according to trader feedback and market conditions. Rh points will be released non-linearly.
    
*   Only traders who meet all the requirements are considered qualified.
    
*   The 1.1x Rh points boost and BonusUSD reward are limited to one entry per trader. Bot registered accounts will not be eligible for rewards.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to disqualify trades that are deemed to be wash trades, displaying attributes of market manipulation, bulk-account registrations to farm additional bonuses or any other attempts at fraud.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to cancel or amend any Activity or Activity Rules at our sole discretion.
    
*   Aster reserves the right of final interpretation of this Activity.
    

Risk Warning: Perpetual trading carries a substantial risk. All trading activities are done at your discretion and at your own risk. The information here should not be regarded as financial or investment advice from Aster. Aster will not be liable for any loss that might arise from your use of Aster.

*   Represents all the yield of the asset.

*   The LP token you get after adding liquidity.

# PancakeSwap | Aster

**Page Summary**

[1\. Mint & Hold asToken StableSwap LPs](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap#id-1.-mint-and-hold-astoken-stableswap-lps)

[2\. Stake StableSwap LPs](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap#c05a)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap#id-1.-mint-and-hold-astoken-stableswap-lps)

1\. Mint & Hold asToken StableSwap LPs


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Earn Au points for minting & holding [**StableSwap LP**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)
 **tokens**.

*   **If you mint V3 LP tokens, you do not get Au points.**
    
*   **Minting StableSwap LP is NOT the same as LP staking.**
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fu9r8XjE4zgXb2G9I0dTz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d5dbf52-ddd5-4d5c-8b9d-9d0670c29be9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfc010c0&sv=2)

*   USDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 35x Au
    
*   asUSDF/USDF StableSwap LP: 30x Au
    
*   asUSDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 25x Au
    
*   asCAKE/CAKE StableSwap LP: 2x Au
    

**How is Au calculated?**

Au points are accrued based on the USD value of the StableSwap LP tokens minted. For example, if you add liquidity to the asUSDF/USDT stable LP on PancakeSwap, which has a 25x Au multiplier, and minted 20 USD worth of stable LP tokens, you should get 20 x 25 = 500 Au. You will continue earning 500 Au/hour.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap#c05a)

2\. Stake StableSwap LPs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Please note that LP Staking is NOT the same as minting & holding** [**StableSwap LPs**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)
**. LP Staking is only available for the following StableSwap pairs:**

*   USDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 35x Au + APR
    
*   asUSDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 25x Au + APR
    

**How do I stake my StableSwap LP?**

Please connect your wallet to PancakeSwap and go to \[My Positions\]. If you already hold StableSwap LPs, click \[Stake LP\] and confirm.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FUTCxjGjjcyaHzeRWwOO6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9bda713-081b-4ed5-a8c9-7107deb21989&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a5ceec4&sv=2)

**How is Au calculated?**

Au multiplier for staking a StableSwap LP is the same as the multiplier for minting and holding. For example, minting and holding asUSDF/USDT stable LP has a 25x Au multiplier. Staking asUSDF/USDT stable LP thus also has a 25x Au multiplier.

Scenario:

*   If you have 20 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP and staked all of it, you continue earning 20 x 25 = 500 Au/hour.
    
*   If you stake 10 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP and continue holding 10 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP, you will earn 10 x 25 = 250 Au/hour from staking and 10 x 25 = 250 Au/hour from holding.
    

**What does APR consist of?**

When you stake StableSwap LPs on PancakeSwap, you also earn Combined APR in the form of CAKE tokens. Combined APR consists of Farm APR and LP fee APR. Please read this for more details about Farm APR: [https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/yield-farmingarrow-up-right](https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/yield-farming)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FMQOVMQCcaSvGufc8sGRH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6e0cc3d-75df-42af-af00-b876b2640643&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7e5b5bf&sv=2)

**How do I collect CAKE token rewards?**

Go to your staked positions and click \[Harvest\] to collect CAKE rewards.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FYeN7pXcf7t2e1mmqJbKO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6000a0b-2966-4f04-9de4-6713234361bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=545bad27&sv=2)

A. Mint & Hold asTokens


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Enjoy up to 10x Au multiplier when you mint & hold asBTC, asUSDF, asBNB or asCAKE on AsterEarn**. Au points stack hourly.

asTokens are liquid staking derivatives of mainstream assets like BTC, BNB, and more. Aside from Au, asTokens earns you multiple sources of real yield!

asBTC

1x

B. Mint & Hold USDF


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Enjoy 20x Au multiplier in S1 when you mint & hold USDF.** Au points stack hourly.

**Enjoy 25x Au multiplier in S1 when you deposit USDF into your Aster Pro mode wallet.** Au points stack houdly.

USDF is a yield-bearing stablecoin backed by crypto assets and corresponding short futures positions. Fund security is prioritized through Ceffu, a trusted third-party custodian, and stringent risk control measures ensure safety.

[**👉 Mint USDF**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/usdf)

C. Mint & Hold ALP


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Get 5x Au multiplier in S1 when you mint & hold ALP**. Au points stack hourly.

ALP provides liquidity for all trading pairs on AsterEX Simple Mode, our on-chain perpetual trading platform supporting multi-asset collateral and high leverage. By minting ALP, liquidity providers participate in market-making. Aside from Au, you also earn platform trading income!

**👉** [**Mint ALP**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[LP on PancakeSwapchevron-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/earn/overview/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/mint-to-earn-au#d048)

E. Au Points Calculation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We take hourly snapshots to calculate Au points. Check your Au points on the [S1 Landing Pagearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
. There is an hourly cap of 100M Au points per address in Stage 1 (Does not include team boost and ref bonus).

**The formula for calculating Au points is:**

**Au = SUM( holding\_token\_USD\_value \* token\_AU\_multiplier ) \* (team boost + Trader boost) + ref bonus**

*   **Au** is the total airdrop points you get from minting and holding assets
    
*   **holding\_token\_USD\_value** refers to the USD investment of your underlying asset. For example, if you stake 0.5 BNB when BNB price is $670, your holding\_token\_USD\_value is 0.5 x 670.
    
*   **token\_AU\_multiplier** is the Au multiplier of the asset. For example, asBNB has a 5x Au multiplier.
    
*   **team boost** is the boost leverage of your team.
    
*   **Trader Boost** is the additional Au boost you earn from trading on Aster Pro mode.
    
*   **ref bonus** is the total Au points you have earned from your Tier 1 and 2 referrals.
    

Scenario:

If you stake 0.5 BNB when BNB price is $670, and asBNB Au multiplier is 5x, your mint earns (0.5 x 670 x 5) = 1,675 Au.

If there is no change in BNB price, you will continue earning (0.5 x 670 x 5) Au per hour.

If BNB price later drops to $650, you will earn (0.5 x 650 x 5) Au per hour.

Last updated 9 months ago

# Treasure Boost Campaign | Aster

We've launched the Treasure Boost campaign for Hyperliquid, GMX, and Drift users. Eligible users can receive either a 1.1x Rh boost **AND/OR** 100 BonusUSD.

**👉** [**Check your eligibility here**arrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/rewards)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/treasure-boost-campaign#id-1.-do-you-qualify-for-extra-1.1x-rh-points-boost-and-or-bonususd)

1\. Do you qualify for extra 1.1x Rh points boost and/or BONUSUSD?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FCNPMAR8bXMBFVefYkBxg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ebceb66-a782-4ce1-adaf-157a43b09685&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b513683&sv=2)

**1.1x Rh points boost**:

*   The points boost is applicable for 30 days after claiming. It will apply to all Aster Pro mode trades made by your wallet.
    
*   For example, if you earned 1000 Rh points from your Pro mode trades, you will get 1000\*1.1 = 1100 Rh points after the boost.
    
*   If you also join a team with e.g. a 1.2x Rh boost, you will get 1000\*（1.2+0.1）= 1300 Rh points after the boost.
    

(If you don't qualify for the extra 1.1x Rh points boost, you can still get up to 1.2x Rh boost by joining a team. See [Referral Bonus & Team Boostsarrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts)
)

**100 BonusUSD**:

*   _**BonusUSD is a unique bonus token on Aster which can be used as collateral when trading perpetuals on Aster Pro mode (BNB Chain).**_
    
*   _**Multi-assets mode has to be activated to use BonusUSD as collateral.**_
    
*   _**BonusUSD can only be used on Aster. It cannot be withdrawn.**_
    
*   _**Profits generated from trades using BonusUSD as collateral can be withdrawn.**_
    

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/treasure-boost-campaign#id-2.-how-to-claim-extra-1.1x-rh-points-boost-and-or-bonususd)

2\. How to claim extra 1.1x Rh points boost and/or BONUSUSD?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to the rewards claim page (coming soon) and connect your wallet. Click \[Claim Reward\] to check your eligibility and claim rewards.

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/treasure-boost-campaign#id-3.-how-to-use-the-bonususd)

3\. How to use the BONUSUSD?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Aster has launched a futures bonus token (BONUSUSD) for users who trade on [Aster Pro Modearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
. BONUSUSD is a futures bonus token issued by Aster. BONUSUSD is a unique USD-pegged token which traders can use as collateral to trade crypto futures on [Aster Pro Modearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
!

_Note: BONUSUSD is a futures bonus token and cannot be withdrawn._ [_Multi-assets mode_arrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro-mode/muti-single-asset-margin)
 _has to be activated to use BONUSUSD as collateral._

**How-to Guide**

Step 1: Go to Campaign page and connect your wallet. Click \[Claim Reward\] to check your eligibility and claim rewards.

Your BONUSUSD tokens will have been automatically credited to your balance after you claim the BONUSUSD manually.

Step 2: Go to the [Portfolioarrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/portfolio)
 and check your BONUSUSD balance.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fi175RG0UBR1bCafwt1hQ%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.49.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61b87967-22b8-4b0d-aeb5-f1d7691a2f28&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a842c9f4&sv=2)

Step 3: (Skip this step if multi-asset mode is already enabled.) Enable [Multi-Assets Modearrow-up-right](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro-mode/muti-single-asset-margin)
 to use BONUSUSD as collateral. On the Aster Pro mode scroll down to ‘Margin Ratio’ & select \[Multi-Assets Mode\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2fQMS9hmvmRtLiiXf9bl%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.51.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0620aff9-2fca-4b37-98b8-08a4c256818a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5c646fc&sv=2)

Step 4: Choose the preferred perpetual contract from the dropdown list. Set your preferred leverage.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FD3GYGsEh9ZYasJu8gku7%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.54.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debe03192-3d26-4fc2-8d84-ed6edc2fc335&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74993da8&sv=2)

Step 5: Set your preferred order type. Aster Pro Mode offers Limit, Market, Stop Limit orders and Trailing Stop order.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FW78kc6RAOagPkg7DiWD8%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.57.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ff1b893-f5a7-48e9-9850-61b43c175368&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=352e713f&sv=2)

Step 6: Monitor your position(s) and close them based on your exit strategy. All your positions are listed in the \[Positions\] tab.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FRj7efFgOK66LTiR9SAm5%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.59.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1bed715e-bc6e-4532-acf1-3d2bd3cc2ca9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87c00e79&sv=2)

# Referral bonus & Team boosts | Aster

**Page summary:**

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#a205)

**1\. How to generate invite code**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to the [S1 landing pagearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
. Connect your wallet. Your invite code will be automatically displayed. Share the code with your invitees. You can also change your name by clicking on the edit button.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmiro.medium.com%2Fv2%2Fresize%3Afit%3A630%2F0*ZXCf2v3uRs_NC0dq&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6310379&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#a205-1)

**2\. How to bind invite code**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to the [S1 landing pagearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
. A screen will pop up to prompt you to enter your invite code. Click \[Redeem invite code\]. Click \[Skip\] if you don’t have one.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmiro.medium.com%2Fv2%2Fresize%3Afit%3A630%2F1*zOZtyD_kWb3BlPP5JEHXUw.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f9d8792&sv=2)

You may also bind an invite code manually. First, go to the [S1 landing pagearrow-up-right](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
 and connect your wallet. Click \[Bind your invite code quickly\]. Enter your inviter’s code. Once done, you will see yourself in the Inviter Team.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmiro.medium.com%2Fv2%2Fresize%3Afit%3A630%2F0*rApYV3W3oeql6Ec0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27c7c4a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmiro.medium.com%2Fv2%2Fresize%3Afit%3A630%2F0*06OWHvA9XlrfZ0D8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=365871ec&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#bb38)

3a. Au referral bonus


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Important notice: The Au Points Program is ending with a final snapshot of Au points balance taken at 00:00 UTC, June 13 2025.**

*   Tier 1 referral: Get 10% of your invitees’ Au points when they mint asTokens, USDF and/or ALP. **Your invitees must bind your invite code before their first mint**.
    
*   Tier 2 referral: Get 5% when your invitees refer their friends to mint asTokens, USDF and/or ALP. **Your invitee’s friends must bind your invitee’s code before their first mint**.
    

**Scenario:**

Alice invites Ben. Ben binds Alice’s invite code.

*   Ben earns 5,000 Au from his first mint.
    
*   Alice earns 10% of Ben’s points. Thus, she gets 5,000\*0.1 = 500 Au.
    

Ben invites Charlie to Aster. Charlie binds Ben’s invite code.

*   Charlie earns 2,500 Au from his first mint.
    
*   Ben earns 10% of Charlie’s points. Thus, he gets 2,500\*0.1 = 250 Au.
    
*   Alice earns 5% of Charlie’s points. Thus, she gets 2,500\*0.05 = 125 Au.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmiro.medium.com%2Fv2%2Fresize%3Afit%3A630%2F1*fvfLyPCwW9I7d4nf1oRe4w.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ed4ac9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#bb38-1)

3b. Au team boost


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Important notice: The Au Points Program is ending with a final snapshot of Au points balance taken at 00:00 UTC, June 13 2025.**

Everyone in a referral family is a Team. Teams can enjoy team boosts. A team is composed of the following members:

*   **The person who invited you (A)**
    
*   **Other invitees of the person who invited you (B)**
    
*   **Yourself (C)**
    
*   **Your invitees (D)**
    

For example, Alice invited you and Don to Aster. You invited Charlie. Charlie invited Evan. Hence, Alice is A. Don is B. You are C. Charlie is D. Evan is not included in your Team.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#eabd)

Team boost scenario:

Team boosts are applied to the **team’s cumulative Au from minting asTokens, USDF and ALP only in the previous hour**. Hourly snapshots are taken to calculate Team Au points. Au earned from referral bonuses or previous team boosts are not included in the total Au amount.

For example:

Alice, Ben and Don are a team. In the previous hour, Alice earned 500,000 Au, Ben earned 300,000 Au and Don earned 200,000 Au. These Au points are earned from minting asTokens, USDF and ALP only. Au earned from their referral bonuses or previous team boosts are not counted.

Team Au in the previous hour = 500,000 + 300,000 + 200,000 = 1,000,000 Au

According to the table below, all members benefit from a 1.05x team boost.

Alice gets 500,000\*1.05 = 525,000 Au. Ben gets 300,000\*1.05 = 315,000 Au. Dion gets 200,000\*1.05 = 210,000 Au.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#id-6511)

**Au team boost:**

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FKqYCPYj1wgBaU5dwshrY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6c94326-fc54-4824-9105-5710612c1ad3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4557cbc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#id-5c12)

4a. Rh referral bonus


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Important Notice: The Stage 1 Rh Points Program has ended with Epoch 21 on June 22, 2025, 23:59 UTC+0, and distribution of Stage 1 Rh points has stopped.**

*   Tier 1 referral: Get 10% of your invitees’ Rh points when they trade on Aster Pro Mode. **Your invitees must bind your invite code before their first trade**.
    
*   Tier 2 referral: Get 5% when your invitees refer their friends to trade. **Your invitee’s friends must bind your invitee’s invite code before their first trade**.
    

**Scenario:**

Wyn invites Yuki to trade on Aster Pro Mode. Yuki binds Wyn’s invite code.

*   Yuki trades 5,000 USD volume. She earns 5,000 Rh.
    
*   Wyn earns 10% of Yuki’s points. Thus, she gets 5,000\*0.1 = 500 Rh.
    

Yuki invites Zen to trade on Aster Pro Mode. Zen binds Yuki’s invite code.

*   Zen trades 2,000 USD volume. Zen earns 2,000 Rh.
    
*   Yuki earns 10% of Zen’s points. Thus, she gets 2,000\*0.1 = 200 Rh.
    
*   Wyn earns 5% of Zen’s points. Thus, she gets 2,000\*0.05 = 100 Rh.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fmiro.medium.com%2Fv2%2Fresize%3Afit%3A630%2F1*paa3Sccw_-g1CMGCWpbEkg.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6685485&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#id-9c09)

4b. Rh team boost


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Everyone in a referral family is a team. Teams can enjoy team boosts. A team is composed of the following members:

*   **The person who invited you (A)**
    
*   **Other invitees of the person who invited you (B)**
    
*   **Yourself (C )**
    
*   **Your invitees (D)**
    

For example: Yuki invited you and Wyn to Aster. You invited Zen, and Zen invited Ben.

*   Yuki = A
    
*   Wyn = B
    
*   You = C
    
*   Zen = D
    
*   Ben is not part of your team because he is a referral of your referral (second level).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#how-team-boosts-work)

How team boosts work

*   Team boosts are based on the team’s cumulative Rh earned from trading on Aster Pro in the previous day.
    
*   Daily snapshots are taken to calculate team Rh points.
    
*   Rh from referral bonuses or previous team boosts are not included.
    

**Example**

Wyn, Yuki, and Zen are a team. On the previous day, they earned:

*   Wyn: 600,000 Rh
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 Rh
    
*   Zen: 100,000 Rh
    

Team Rh = 600,000 + 300,000 + 100,000 = 1,000,000 Rh

According to the boost table, the team qualifies for a 1.05x boost, applied equally to each member’s Rh:

*   Wyn: 600,000 × 1.05 = 630,000 Rh
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 × 1.05 = 315,000 Rh
    
*   Zen: 100,000 × 1.05 = 105,000 Rh
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#id-87af)
